provided\")\n   184→\t}\n   185→\tif pool == nil {\n   186→\t\tpool = chunkenc.NewPool()\n   187→\t}\n   188→\tif l == nil {\n   189→\t\tl = log.NewNopLogger()\n   190→\t}\n   191→\tmergeFunc := opts.MergeFunc\n   192→\tif mergeFunc == nil {\n   193→\t\tmergeFunc = storage.NewCompactingChunkSeriesMerger(storage.ChainedSeriesMerge)\n   194→\t}\n   195→\tmaxBlockChunkSegmentSize := opts.MaxBlockChunkSegmentSize\n   196→\tif maxBlockChunkSegmentSize == 0 {\n   197→\t\tmaxBlockChunkSegmentSize = chunks.DefaultChunkSegmentSize\n   198→\t}\n   199→\tpe := opts.PE\n   200→\tif pe == nil {\n   201→\t\tpe = index.EncodePostingsRaw\n   202→\t}\n   203→\treturn &LeveledCompactor{\n   204→\t\tranges:                      ranges,\n   205→\t\tchunkPool:                   pool,\n   206→\t\tlogger:                      l,\n   207→\t\tmetrics:                     NewCompactorMetrics(r),\n   208→\t\tctx:                         ctx,\n   209→\t\tmaxBlockChunkSegmentSize:    maxBlockChunkSegmentSize,\n   210→\t\tmergeFunc:                   mergeFunc,\n   211→\t\tpostingsEncoder:             pe,\n   212→\t\tenableOverlappingCompaction: opts.EnableOverlappingCompaction,\n   213→\t}, nil\n   214→}\n   215→\n   216→type dirMeta struct {\n   217→\tdir  string\n   218→\tmeta *BlockMeta\n   219→}\n   220→\n   221→// Plan returns a list of compactable blocks in the provided directory.\n   222→func (c *LeveledCompactor) Plan(dir string) ([]string, error) {\n   223→\tdirs, err := blockDirs(dir)\n   224→\tif err != nil {\n   225→\t\treturn nil, err\n   226→\t}\n   227→\tif len(dirs) < 1 {\n   228→\t\treturn nil, nil\n   229→\t}\n   230→\n   231→\tvar dms []dirMeta\n   232→\tfor _, dir := range dirs {\n   233→\t\tmeta, _, err := readMetaFile(dir)\n   234→\t\tif err != nil {\n   235→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   236→\t\t}\n   237→\t\tdms = append(dms, dirMeta{dir, meta})\n   238→\t}\n   239→\treturn c.plan(dms)\n   240→}\n   241→\n   242→func (c *LeveledCompactor) plan(dms []dirMeta) ([]string, error) {\n   243→\tslices.SortFunc(dms, func(a, b dirMeta) int {\n   244→\t\tswitch {\n   245→\t\tcase a.meta.MinTime < b.meta.MinTime:\n   246→\t\t\treturn -1\n   247→\t\tcase a.meta.MinTime > b.meta.MinTime:\n   248→\t\t\treturn 1\n   249→\t\tdefault:\n   250→\t\t\treturn 0\n   251→\t\t}\n   252→\t})\n   253→\n   254→\tres := c.selectOverlappingDirs(dms)\n   255→\tif len(res) > 0 {\n   256→\t\treturn res, nil\n   257→\t}\n   258→\t// No overlapping blocks, do compaction the usual way.\n   259→\t// We do not include a recently created block with max(minTime), so the block which was just created from WAL.\n   260→\t// This gives users a window of a full block size to piece-wise backup new data without having to care about data overlap.\n   261→\tdms = dms[:len(dms)-1]\n   262→\n   263→\tfor _, dm := range c.selectDirs(dms) {\n   264→\t\tres = append(res, dm.dir)\n   265→\t}\n   266→\tif len(res) > 0 {\n   267→\t\treturn res, nil\n   268→\t}\n   269→\n   270→\t// Compact any blocks with big enough time range that have >5% tombstones.\n   271→\tfor i := len(dms) - 1; i >= 0; i-- {\n   272→\t\tmeta := dms[i].meta\n   273→\t\tif meta.MaxTime-meta.MinTime < c.ranges[len(c.ranges)/2] {\n   274→\t\t\t// If the block is entirely deleted, then we don't care about the block being big enough.\n   275→\t\t\t// TODO: This is assuming single tombstone is for distinct series, which might be no true.\n   276→\t\t\tif meta.Stats.NumTombstones > 0 && meta.Stats.NumTombstones >= meta.Stats.NumSeries {\n   277→\t\t\t\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\n   278→\t\t\t}\n   279→\t\t\tbreak\n   280→\t\t}\n   281→\t\tif float64(meta.Stats.NumTombstones)/float64(meta.Stats.NumSeries+1) > 0.05 {\n   282→\t\t\treturn []string{dms[i].dir}, nil\n   283→\t\t}\n   284→\t}\n   285→\n   286→\treturn nil, nil\n   287→}\n   288→\n   289→// selectDirs returns the dir metas that should be compacted into a single new block.\n   290→// If only a single block range is configured, the result is always nil.\n   291→func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectDirs(ds []dirMeta) []dirMeta {\n   292→\tif len(c.ranges) < 2 || len(ds) < 1 {\n   293→\t\treturn nil\n   294→\t}\n   295→\n   296→\thighTime := ds[len(ds)-1].meta.MinTime\n   297→\n   298→\tfor _, iv := range c.ranges[1:] {\n   299→\t\tparts := splitByRange(ds, iv)\n   300→\t\tif len(parts) == 0 {\n   301→\t\t\tcontinue\n   302→\t\t}\n   303→\n   304→\tOuter:\n   305→\t\tfor _, p := range parts {\n   306→\t\t\t// Do not select the range if it has a block whose compaction failed.\n   307→\t\t\tfor _, dm := range p {\n   308→\t\t\t\tif dm.meta.Compaction.Failed {\n   309→\t\t\t\t\tcontinue Outer\n   310→\t\t\t\t}\n   311→\t\t\t}\n   312→\n   313→\t\t\tmint := p[0].meta.MinTime\n   314→\t\t\tmaxt := p[len(p)-1].meta.MaxTime\n   315→\t\t\t// Pick the range of blocks if it spans the full range (potentially with gaps)\n   316→\t\t\t// or is before the most recent block.\n   317→\t\t\t// This ensures we don't compact blocks prematurely when another one of the same\n   318→\t\t\t// size still fits in the range.\n   319→\t\t\tif (maxt-mint == iv || maxt <= highTime) && len(p) > 1 {\n   320→\t\t\t\treturn p\n   321→\t\t\t}\n   322→\t\t}\n   323→\t}\n   324→\n   325→\treturn nil\n   326→}\n   327→\n   328→// selectOverlappingDirs returns all dirs with overlapping time ranges.\n   329→// It expects sorted input by mint and returns the overlapping dirs in the same order as received.\n   330→func (c *LeveledCompactor) selectOverlappingDirs(ds []dirMeta) []string {\n   331→\tif !c.enableOverlappingCompaction {\n   332→\t\treturn nil\n   333→\t}\n   334→\tif len(ds) < 2 {\n   335→\t\treturn nil\n   336→\t}\n   337→\tvar overlappingDirs []string\n   338→\tglobalMaxt := ds[0].meta.MaxTime\n   339→\tfor i, d := range ds[1:] {\n   340→\t\tif d.meta.MinTime < globalMaxt {\n   341→\t\t\tif len(overlappingDirs) == 0 { // When it is the first overlap, need to add the last one as well.\n   342→\t\t\t\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, ds[i].dir)\n   343→\t\t\t}\n   344→\t\t\toverlappingDirs = append(overlappingDirs, d.dir)\n   345→\t\t} else if len(overlappingDirs) > 0 {\n   346→\t\t\tbreak\n   347→\t\t}\n   348→\t\tif d.meta.MaxTime > globalMaxt {\n   349→\t\t\tglobalMaxt = d.meta.MaxTime\n   350→\t\t}\n   351→\t}\n   352→\treturn overlappingDirs\n   353→}\n   354→\n   355→// splitByRange splits the directories by the time range. The range sequence starts at 0.\n   356→//\n   357→// For example, if we have blocks [0-10, 10-20, 50-60, 90-100] and the split range tr is 30\n   358→// it returns [0-10, 10-20], [50-60], [90-100].\n   359→func splitByRange(ds []dirMeta, tr int64) [][]dirMeta {\n   360→\tvar splitDirs [][]dirMeta\n   361→\n   362→\tfor i := 0; i < len(ds); {\n   363→\t\tvar (\n   364→\t\t\tgroup []dirMeta\n   365→\t\t\tt0    int64\n   366→\t\t\tm     = ds[i].meta\n   367→\t\t)\n   368→\t\t// Compute start of aligned time range of size tr closest to the current block's start.\n   369→\t\tif m.MinTime >= 0 {\n   370→\t\t\tt0 = tr * (m.MinTime / tr)\n   371→\t\t} else {\n   372→\t\t\tt0 = tr * ((m.MinTime - tr + 1) / tr)\n   373→\t\t}\n   374→\t\t// Skip blocks that don't fall into the range. This can happen via mis-alignment or\n   375→\t\t// by being the multiple of the intended range.\n   376→\t\tif m.MaxTime > t0+tr {\n   377→\t\t\ti++\n   378→\t\t\tcontinue\n   379→\t\t}\n   380→\n   381→\t\t// Add all dirs to the current group that are within [t0, t0+tr].\n   382→\t\tfor ; i < len(ds); i++ {\n   383→\t\t\t// Either the block falls into the next range or doesn't fit at all (checked above).\n   384→\t\t\tif ds[i].meta.MaxTime > t0+tr {\n   385→\t\t\t\tbreak\n   386→\t\t\t}\n   387→\t\t\tgroup = append(group, ds[i])\n   388→\t\t}\n   389→\n   390→\t\tif len(group) > 0 {\n   391→\t\t\tsplitDirs = append(splitDirs, group)\n   392→\t\t}\n   393→\t}\n   394→\n   395→\treturn splitDirs\n   396→}\n   397→\n   398→// CompactBlockMetas merges many block metas into one, combining it's source blocks together\n   399→// and adjusting compaction level. Min/Max time of result block meta covers all input blocks.\n   400→func CompactBlockMetas(uid ulid.ULID, blocks ...*BlockMeta) *BlockMeta {\n   401→\tres := &BlockMeta{\n   402→\t\tULID: uid,\n   403→\t}\n   404→\n   405→\tsources := map[ulid.ULID]struct{}{}\n   406→\tmint := blocks[0].MinTime\n   407→\tmaxt := blocks[0].MaxTime\n   408→\n   409→\tfor _, b := range blocks {\n   410→\t\tif b.MinTime < mint {\n   411→\t\t\tmint = b.MinTime\n   412→\t\t}\n   413→\t\tif b.MaxTime > maxt {\n   414→\t\t\tmaxt = b.MaxTime\n   415→\t\t}\n   416→\t\tif b.Compaction.Level > res.Compaction.Level {\n   417→\t\t\tres.Compaction.Level = b.Compaction.Level\n   418→\t\t}\n   419→\t\tfor _, s := range b.Compaction.Sources {\n   420→\t\t\tsources[s] = struct{}{}\n   421→\t\t}\n   422→\t\tres.Compaction.Parents = append(res.Compaction.Parents, BlockDesc{\n   423→\t\t\tULID:    b.ULID,\n   424→\t\t\tMinTime: b.MinTime,\n   425→\t\t\tMaxTime: b.MaxTime,\n   426→\t\t})\n   427→\t}\n   428→\tres.Compaction.Level++\n   429→\n   430→\tfor s := range sources {\n   431→\t\tres.Compaction.Sources = append(res.Compaction.Sources, s)\n   432→\t}\n   433→\tslices.SortFunc(res.Compaction.Sources, func(a, b ulid.ULID) int {\n   434→\t\treturn a.Compare(b)\n   435→\t})\n   436→\n   437→\tres.MinTime = mint\n   438→\tres.MaxTime = maxt\n   439→\treturn res\n   440→}\n   441→\n   442→// Compact creates a new block in the compactor's directory from the blocks in the\n   443→// provided directories.\n   444→func (c *LeveledCompactor) Compact(dest string, dirs []string, open []*Block) (uid ulid.ULID, err error) {\n   445→\treturn c.CompactWithBlockPopulator(dest, dirs, open, DefaultBlockPopulator{})\n   446→}\n   447→\n   448→func (c *LeveledCompactor) CompactWithBlockPopulator(dest string, dirs []string, open []*Block, blockPopulator BlockPopulator) (uid ulid.ULID, err error) {\n   449→\tvar (\n   450→\t\tblocks []BlockReader\n   451→\t\tbs     []*Block\n   452→\t\tmetas  []*BlockMeta\n   453→\t\tuids   []string\n   454→\t)\n   455→\tstart := time.Now()\n   456→\n   457→\tfor _, d := range dirs {\n   458→\t\tmeta, _, err := readMetaFile(d)\n   459→\t\tif err != nil {\n   460→\t\t\treturn uid, err\n   461→\t\t}\n   462→\n   463→\t\tvar b *Block\n   464→\n   465→\t\t// Use already open blocks if we can, to avoid\n   466→\t\t// having the index data in memory twice.\n   467→\t\tfor _, o := range open {\n   468→\t\t\tif meta.ULID == o.Meta().ULID {\n   469→\t\t\t\tb = o\n   470→\t\t\t\tbreak\n   471→\t\t\t}\n   472→\t\t}\n   473→\n   474→\t\tif b == nil {\n   475→\t\t\tvar err error\n   476→\t\t\tb, err = OpenBlock(c.logger, d, c.chunkPool)\n   477→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   478→\t\t\t\treturn uid, err\n   479→\t\t\t}\n   480→\t\t\tdefer b.Close()\n   481→\t\t}\n   482→\n   483→\t\tmetas = append(metas, meta)\n   484→\t\tblocks = append(blocks, b)\n   485→\t\tbs = append(bs, b)\n   486→\t\tuids = append(uids, meta.ULID.String())\n   487→\t}\n   488→\n   489→\tuid = ulid.MustNew(ulid.Now(), rand.Reader)\n   490→\n   491→\tmeta := CompactBlockMetas(uid, metas...)\n   492→\terr = c.write(dest, meta, blockPopulator, blocks...)\n   493→\tif err == nil {\n   494→\t\tif meta.Stats.NumSamples == 0 {\n   495→\t\t\tfor _, b := range bs {\n   496→\t\t\t\tb.meta.Compaction.Deletable = true\n   497→\t\t\t\tn, err := writeMetaFile(c.logger, b.dir, &b.meta)\n   498→\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   499→\t\t\t\t\tlevel.Error(c.logger).Log(\n   500→\t\t\t\t\t\t\"msg\", \"Failed to write 'Deletable' to meta file after compaction\",\n   501→\t\t\t\t\t\t\"ulid\", b.meta.ULID,\n   502→\t\t\t\t\t)\n   503→\t\t\t\t}\n   504→\t\t\t\tb.numBytesMeta = n\n   505→\t\t\t}\n   506→\t\t\tuid = ulid.ULID{}\n   507→\t\t\tlevel.Info(c.logger).Log(\n   508→\t\t\t\t\"msg\", \"compact blocks resulted in empty block\",\n   509→\t\t\t\t\"count\", len(blocks),\n   510→\t\t\t\t\"sources\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", uids),\n   511→\t\t\t\t\"duration\", time.Since(start),\n   512→\t\t\t)\n   513→\t\t} else {\n   514→\t\t\tlevel.Info(c.logger).Log(\n   515→\t\t\t\t\"msg\", \"compact blocks\",\n   516→\t\t\t\t\"count\", len(blocks),\n   517→\t\t\t\t\"mint\", meta.MinTime,\n   518→\t\t\t\t\"maxt\", meta.MaxTime,\n   519→\t\t\t\t\"ulid\", meta.ULID,\n   520→\t\t\t\t\"sources\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", uids),\n   521→\t\t\t\t\"duration\", time.Since(start),\n   522→\t\t\t)\n   523→\t\t}\n   524→\t\treturn uid, nil\n   525→\t}\n   526→\n   527→\terrs := tsdb_errors.NewMulti(err)\n   528→\tif !errors.Is(err, context.Canceled) {\n   529→\t\tfor _, b := range bs {\n   530→\t\t\tif err := b.setCompactionFailed(); err != nil {\n   531→\t\t\t\terrs.Add(fmt.Errorf(\"setting compaction failed for block: %s: %w\", b.Dir(), err))\n   532→\t\t\t}\n   533→\t\t}\n   534→\t}\n   535→\n   536→\treturn uid, errs.Err()\n   537→}\n   538→\n   539→func (c *LeveledCompactor) Write(dest string, b BlockReader, mint, maxt int64, base *BlockMeta) (ulid.ULID, error) {\n   540→\tstart := time.Now()\n   541→\n   542→\tuid := ulid.MustNew(ulid.Now(), rand.Reader)\n   543→\n   544→\tmeta := &BlockMeta{\n   545→\t\tULID:    uid,\n   546→\t\tMinTime: mint,\n   547→\t\tMaxTime: maxt,\n   548→\t}\n   549→\tmeta.Compaction.Level = 1\n   550→\tmeta.Compaction.Sources = []ulid.ULID{uid}\n   551→\n   552→\tif base != nil {\n   553→\t\tmeta.Compaction.Parents = []BlockDesc{\n   554→\t\t\t{ULID: base.ULID, MinTime: base.MinTime, MaxTime: base.MaxTime},\n   555→\t\t}\n   556→\t\tif base.Compaction.FromOutOfOrder() {\n   557→\t\t\tmeta.Compaction.SetOutOfOrder()\n   558→\t\t}\n   559→\t}\n   560→\n   561→\terr := c.write(dest, meta, DefaultBlockPopulator{}, b)\n   562→\tif err != nil {\n   563→\t\treturn uid, err\n   564→\t}\n   565→\n   566→\tif meta.Stats.NumSamples == 0 {\n   567→\t\tlevel.Info(c.logger).Log(\n   568→\t\t\t\"msg\", \"write block resulted in empty block\",\n   569→\t\t\t\"mint\", meta.MinTime,\n   570→\t\t\t\"maxt\", meta.MaxTime,\n   571→\t\t\t\"duration\", time.Since(start),\n   572→\t\t)\n   573→\t\treturn ulid.ULID{}, nil\n   574→\t}\n   575→\n   576→\tlevel.Info(c.logger).Log(\n   577→\t\t\"msg\", \"write block\",\n   578→\t\t\"mint\", meta.MinTime,\n   579→\t\t\"maxt\", meta.MaxTime,\n   580→\t\t\"ulid\", meta.ULID,\n   581→\t\t\"duration\", time.Since(start),\n   582→\t\t\"ooo\", meta.Compaction.FromOutOfOrder(),\n   583→\t)\n   584→\treturn uid, nil\n   585→}\n   586→\n   587→// instrumentedChunkWriter is used for level 1 compactions to record statistics\n   588→// about compacted chunks.\n   589→type instrumentedChunkWriter struct {\n   590→\tChunkWriter\n   591→\n   592→\tsize    prometheus.Histogram\n   593→\tsamples prometheus.Histogram\n   594→\ttrange  prometheus.Histogram\n   595→}\n   596→\n   597→func (w *instrumentedChunkWriter) WriteChunks(chunks ...chunks.Meta) error {\n   598→\tfor _, c := range chunks {\n   599→\t\tw.size.Observe(float64(len(c.Chunk.Bytes())))\n   600→\t\tw.samples.Observe(float64(c.Chunk.NumSamples()))\n   601→\t\tw.trange.Observe(float64(c.MaxTime - c.MinTime))\n   602→\t}\n   603→\treturn w.ChunkWriter.WriteChunks(chunks...)\n   604→}\n   605→\n   606→// write creates a new block that is the union of the provided blocks into dir.\n   607→func (c *LeveledCompactor) write(dest string, meta *BlockMeta, blockPopulator BlockPopulator, blocks ...BlockReader) (err error) {\n   608→\tdir := filepath.Join(dest, meta.ULID.String())\n   609→\ttmp := dir + tmpForCreationBlockDirSuffix\n   610→\tvar closers []io.Closer\n   611→\tdefer func(t time.Time) {\n   612→\t\terr = tsdb_errors.NewMulti(err, tsdb_errors.CloseAll(closers)).Err()\n   613→\n   614→\t\t// RemoveAll returns no error when tmp doesn't exist so it is safe to always run it.\n   615→\t\tif err := os.RemoveAll(tmp); err != nil {\n   616→\t\t\tlevel.Error(c.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"removed tmp folder after failed compaction\", \"err\", err.Error())\n   617→\t\t}\n   618→\t\tc.metrics.Ran.Inc()\n   619→\t\tc.metrics.Duration.Observe(time.Since(t).Seconds())\n   620→\t}(time.Now())\n   621→\n   622→\tif err = os.RemoveAll(tmp); err != nil {\n   623→\t\treturn err\n   624→\t}\n   625→\n   626→\tif err = os.MkdirAll(tmp, 0o777); err != nil {\n   627→\t\treturn err\n   628→\t}\n   629→\n   630→\t// Populate chunk and index files into temporary directory with\n   631→\t// data of all blocks.\n   632→\tvar chunkw ChunkWriter\n   633→\n   634→\tchunkw, err = chunks.NewWriterWithSegSize(chunkDir(tmp), c.maxBlockChunkSegmentSize)\n   635→\tif err != nil {\n   636→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"open chunk writer: %w\", err)\n   637→\t}\n   638→\tclosers = append(closers, chunkw)\n   639→\t// Record written chunk sizes on level 1 compactions.\n   640→\tif meta.Compaction.Level == 1 {\n   641→\t\tchunkw = &instrumentedChunkWriter{\n   642→\t\t\tChunkWriter: chunkw,\n   643→\t\t\tsize:        c.metrics.ChunkSize,\n   644→\t\t\tsamples:     c.metrics.ChunkSamples,\n   645→\t\t\ttrange:      c.metrics.ChunkRange,\n   646→\t\t}\n   647→\t}\n   648→\n   649→\tindexw, err := index.NewWriterWithEncoder(c.ctx, filepath.Join(tmp, indexFilename), c.postingsEncoder)\n   650→\tif err != nil {\n   651→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"open index writer: %w\", err)\n   652→\t}\n   653→\tclosers = append(closers, indexw)\n   654→\n   655→\tif err := blockPopulator.PopulateBlock(c.ctx, c.metrics, c.logger, c.chunkPool, c.mergeFunc, blocks, meta, indexw, chunkw); err != nil {\n   656→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"populate block: %w\", err)\n   657→\t}\n   658→\n   659→\tselect {\n   660→\tcase <-c.ctx.Done():\n   661→\t\treturn c.ctx.Err()\n   662→\tdefault:\n   663→\t}\n   664→\n   665→\t// We are explicitly closing them here to check for error even\n   666→\t// though these are covered under defer. This is because in Windows,\n   667→\t// you cannot delete these unless they are closed and the defer is to\n   668→\t// make sure they are closed if the function exits due to an error above.\n   669→\terrs := tsdb_errors.NewMulti()\n   670→\tfor _, w := range closers {\n   671→\t\terrs.Add(w.Close())\n   672→\t}\n   673→\tclosers = closers[:0] // Avoid closing the writers twice in the defer.\n   674→\tif errs.Err() != nil {\n   675→\t\treturn errs.Err()\n   676→\t}\n   677→\n   678→\t// Populated block is empty, so exit early.\n   679→\tif meta.Stats.NumSamples == 0 {\n   680→\t\treturn nil\n   681→\t}\n   682→\n   683→\tif _, err = writeMetaFile(c.logger, tmp, meta); err != nil {\n   684→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"write merged meta: %w\", err)\n   685→\t}\n   686→\n   687→\t// Create an empty tombstones file.\n   688→\tif _, err := tombstones.WriteFile(c.logger, tmp, tombstones.NewMemTombstones()); err != nil {\n   689→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"write new tombstones file: %w\", err)\n   690→\t}\n   691→\n   692→\tdf, err := fileutil.OpenDir(tmp)\n   693→\tif err != nil {\n   694→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"open temporary block dir: %w\", err)\n   695→\t}\n   696→\tdefer func() {\n   697→\t\tif df != nil {\n   698→\t\t\tdf.Close()\n   699→\t\t}\n   700→\t}()\n   701→\n   702→\tif err := df.Sync();
