\"prometheus_tsdb_symbol_table_size_bytes\",\n   274→\t\tHelp: \"Size of symbol table in memory for loaded blocks\",\n   275→\t}, func() float64 {\n   276→\t\tdb.mtx.RLock()\n   277→\t\tblocks := db.blocks\n   278→\t\tdb.mtx.RUnlock()\n   279→\t\tsymTblSize := uint64(0)\n   280→\t\tfor _, b := range blocks {\n   281→\t\t\tsymTblSize += b.GetSymbolTableSize()\n   282→\t\t}\n   283→\t\treturn float64(symTblSize)\n   284→\t})\n   285→\tm.reloads = prometheus.NewCounter(prometheus.CounterOpts{\n   286→\t\tName: \"prometheus_tsdb_reloads_total\",\n   287→\t\tHelp: \"Number of times the database reloaded block data from disk.\",\n   288→\t})\n   289→\tm.reloadsFailed = prometheus.NewCounter(prometheus.CounterOpts{\n   290→\t\tName: \"prometheus_tsdb_reloads_failures_total\",\n   291→\t\tHelp: \"Number of times the database failed to reloadBlocks block data from disk.\",\n   292→\t})\n   293→\tm.compactionsTriggered = prometheus.NewCounter(prometheus.CounterOpts{\n   294→\t\tName: \"prometheus_tsdb_compactions_triggered_total\",\n   295→\t\tHelp: \"Total number of triggered compactions for the partition.\",\n   296→\t})\n   297→\tm.compactionsFailed = prometheus.NewCounter(prometheus.CounterOpts{\n   298→\t\tName: \"prometheus_tsdb_compactions_failed_total\",\n   299→\t\tHelp: \"Total number of compactions that failed for the partition.\",\n   300→\t})\n   301→\tm.timeRetentionCount = prometheus.NewCounter(prometheus.CounterOpts{\n   302→\t\tName: \"prometheus_tsdb_time_retentions_total\",\n   303→\t\tHelp: \"The number of times that blocks were deleted because the maximum time limit was exceeded.\",\n   304→\t})\n   305→\tm.compactionsSkipped = prometheus.NewCounter(prometheus.CounterOpts{\n   306→\t\tName: \"prometheus_tsdb_compactions_skipped_total\",\n   307→\t\tHelp: \"Total number of skipped compactions due to disabled auto compaction.\",\n   308→\t})\n   309→\tm.startTime = prometheus.NewGaugeFunc(prometheus.GaugeOpts{\n   310→\t\tName: \"prometheus_tsdb_lowest_timestamp\",\n   311→\t\tHelp: \"Lowest timestamp value stored in the database. The unit is decided by the library consumer.\",\n   312→\t}, func() float64 {\n   313→\t\tdb.mtx.RLock()\n   314→\t\tdefer db.mtx.RUnlock()\n   315→\t\tif len(db.blocks) == 0 {\n   316→\t\t\treturn float64(db.head.MinTime())\n   317→\t\t}\n   318→\t\treturn float64(db.blocks[0].meta.MinTime)\n   319→\t})\n   320→\tm.tombCleanTimer = prometheus.NewHistogram(prometheus.HistogramOpts{\n   321→\t\tName:                            \"prometheus_tsdb_tombstone_cleanup_seconds\",\n   322→\t\tHelp:                            \"The time taken to recompact blocks to remove tombstones.\",\n   323→\t\tNativeHistogramBucketFactor:     1.1,\n   324→\t\tNativeHistogramMaxBucketNumber:  100,\n   325→\t\tNativeHistogramMinResetDuration: 1 * time.Hour,\n   326→\t})\n   327→\tm.blocksBytes = prometheus.NewGauge(prometheus.GaugeOpts{\n   328→\t\tName: \"prometheus_tsdb_storage_blocks_bytes\",\n   329→\t\tHelp: \"The number of bytes that are currently used for local storage by all blocks.\",\n   330→\t})\n   331→\tm.maxBytes = prometheus.NewGauge(prometheus.GaugeOpts{\n   332→\t\tName: \"prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_bytes\",\n   333→\t\tHelp: \"Max number of bytes to be retained in the tsdb blocks, configured 0 means disabled\",\n   334→\t})\n   335→\tm.retentionDuration = prometheus.NewGauge(prometheus.GaugeOpts{\n   336→\t\tName: \"prometheus_tsdb_retention_limit_seconds\",\n   337→\t\tHelp: \"How long to retain samples in storage.\",\n   338→\t})\n   339→\tm.sizeRetentionCount = prometheus.NewCounter(prometheus.CounterOpts{\n   340→\t\tName: \"prometheus_tsdb_size_retentions_total\",\n   341→\t\tHelp: \"The number of times that blocks were deleted because the maximum number of bytes was exceeded.\",\n   342→\t})\n   343→\n   344→\tif r != nil {\n   345→\t\tr.MustRegister(\n   346→\t\t\tm.loadedBlocks,\n   347→\t\t\tm.symbolTableSize,\n   348→\t\t\tm.reloads,\n   349→\t\t\tm.reloadsFailed,\n   350→\t\t\tm.compactionsFailed,\n   351→\t\t\tm.compactionsTriggered,\n   352→\t\t\tm.compactionsSkipped,\n   353→\t\t\tm.sizeRetentionCount,\n   354→\t\t\tm.timeRetentionCount,\n   355→\t\t\tm.startTime,\n   356→\t\t\tm.tombCleanTimer,\n   357→\t\t\tm.blocksBytes,\n   358→\t\t\tm.maxBytes,\n   359→\t\t\tm.retentionDuration,\n   360→\t\t)\n   361→\t}\n   362→\treturn m\n   363→}\n   364→\n   365→// DBStats contains statistics about the DB separated by component (eg. head).\n   366→// They are available before the DB has finished initializing.\n   367→type DBStats struct {\n   368→\tHead *HeadStats\n   369→}\n   370→\n   371→// NewDBStats returns a new DBStats object initialized using the\n   372→// new function from each component.\n   373→func NewDBStats() *DBStats {\n   374→\treturn &DBStats{\n   375→\t\tHead: NewHeadStats(),\n   376→\t}\n   377→}\n   378→\n   379→// ErrClosed is returned when the db is closed.\n   380→var ErrClosed = errors.New(\"db already closed\")\n   381→\n   382→// DBReadOnly provides APIs for read only operations on a database.\n   383→// Current implementation doesn't support concurrency so\n   384→// all API calls should happen in the same go routine.\n   385→type DBReadOnly struct {\n   386→\tlogger  log.Logger\n   387→\tdir     string\n   388→\tclosers []io.Closer\n   389→\tclosed  chan struct{}\n   390→}\n   391→\n   392→// OpenDBReadOnly opens DB in the given directory for read only operations.\n   393→func OpenDBReadOnly(dir string, l log.Logger) (*DBReadOnly, error) {\n   394→\tif _, err := os.Stat(dir); err != nil {\n   395→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"opening the db dir: %w\", err)\n   396→\t}\n   397→\n   398→\tif l == nil {\n   399→\t\tl = log.NewNopLogger()\n   400→\t}\n   401→\n   402→\treturn &DBReadOnly{\n   403→\t\tlogger: l,\n   404→\t\tdir:    dir,\n   405→\t\tclosed: make(chan struct{}),\n   406→\t}, nil\n   407→}\n   408→\n   409→// FlushWAL creates a new block containing all data that's currently in the memory buffer/WAL.\n   410→// Samples that are in existing blocks will not be written to the new block.\n   411→// Note that if the read only database is running concurrently with a\n   412→// writable database then writing the WAL to the database directory can race.\n   413→func (db *DBReadOnly) FlushWAL(dir string) (returnErr error) {\n   414→\tblockReaders, err := db.Blocks()\n   415→\tif err != nil {\n   416→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"read blocks: %w\", err)\n   417→\t}\n   418→\tmaxBlockTime := int64(math.MinInt64)\n   419→\tif len(blockReaders) > 0 {\n   420→\t\tmaxBlockTime = blockReaders[len(blockReaders)-1].Meta().MaxTime\n   421→\t}\n   422→\tw, err := wlog.Open(db.logger, filepath.Join(db.dir, \"wal\"))\n   423→\tif err != nil {\n   424→\t\treturn err\n   425→\t}\n   426→\tvar wbl *wlog.WL\n   427→\twblDir := filepath.Join(db.dir, wlog.WblDirName)\n   428→\tif _, err := os.Stat(wblDir); !os.IsNotExist(err) {\n   429→\t\twbl, err = wlog.Open(db.logger, wblDir)\n   430→\t\tif err != nil {\n   431→\t\t\treturn err\n   432→\t\t}\n   433→\t}\n   434→\topts := DefaultHeadOptions()\n   435→\topts.ChunkDirRoot = db.dir\n   436→\thead, err := NewHead(nil, db.logger, w, wbl, opts, NewHeadStats())\n   437→\tif err != nil {\n   438→\t\treturn err\n   439→\t}\n   440→\tdefer func() {\n   441→\t\terrs := tsdb_errors.NewMulti(returnErr)\n   442→\t\tif err := head.Close(); err != nil {\n   443→\t\t\terrs.Add(fmt.Errorf(\"closing Head: %w\", err))\n   444→\t\t}\n   445→\t\treturnErr = errs.Err()\n   446→\t}()\n   447→\t// Set the min valid time for the ingested wal samples\n   448→\t// to be no lower than the maxt of the last block.\n   449→\tif err := head.Init(maxBlockTime); err != nil {\n   450→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"read WAL: %w\", err)\n   451→\t}\n   452→\tmint := head.MinTime()\n   453→\tmaxt := head.MaxTime()\n   454→\trh := NewRangeHead(head, mint, maxt)\n   455→\tcompactor, err := NewLeveledCompactor(\n   456→\t\tcontext.Background(),\n   457→\t\tnil,\n   458→\t\tdb.logger,\n   459→\t\tExponentialBlockRanges(DefaultOptions().MinBlockDuration, 3, 5),\n   460→\t\tchunkenc.NewPool(), nil,\n   461→\t)\n   462→\tif err != nil {\n   463→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"create leveled compactor: %w\", err)\n   464→\t}\n   465→\t// Add +1 millisecond to block maxt because block intervals are half-open: [b.MinTime, b.MaxTime).\n   466→\t// Because of this block intervals are always +1 than the total samples it includes.\n   467→\t_, err = compactor.Write(dir, rh, mint, maxt+1, nil)\n   468→\tif err != nil {\n   469→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"writing WAL: %w\", err)\n   470→\t}\n   471→\treturn nil\n   472→}\n   473→\n   474→func (db *DBReadOnly) loadDataAsQueryable(maxt int64) (storage.SampleAndChunkQueryable, error) {\n   475→\tselect {\n   476→\tcase <-db.closed:\n   477→\t\treturn nil, ErrClosed\n   478→\tdefault:\n   479→\t}\n   480→\tblockReaders, err := db.Blocks()\n   481→\tif err != nil {\n   482→\t\treturn nil, err\n   483→\t}\n   484→\tblocks := make([]*Block, len(blockReaders))\n   485→\tfor i, b := range blockReaders {\n   486→\t\tb, ok := b.(*Block)\n   487→\t\tif !ok {\n   488→\t\t\treturn nil, errors.New(\"unable to convert a read only block to a normal block\")\n   489→\t\t}\n   490→\t\tblocks[i] = b\n   491→\t}\n   492→\n   493→\topts := DefaultHeadOptions()\n   494→\topts.ChunkDirRoot = db.dir\n   495→\thead, err := NewHead(nil, db.logger, nil, nil, opts, NewHeadStats())\n   496→\tif err != nil {\n   497→\t\treturn nil, err\n   498→\t}\n   499→\tmaxBlockTime := int64(math.MinInt64)\n   500→\tif len(blocks) > 0 {\n   501→\t\tmaxBlockTime = blocks[len(blocks)-1].Meta().MaxTime\n   502→\t}\n   503→\n   504→\t// Also add the WAL if the current blocks don't cover the requests time range.\n   505→\tif maxBlockTime <= maxt {\n   506→\t\tif err := head.Close(); err != nil {\n   507→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   508→\t\t}\n   509→\t\tw, err := wlog.Open(db.logger, filepath.Join(db.dir, \"wal\"))\n   510→\t\tif err != nil {\n   511→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   512→\t\t}\n   513→\t\tvar wbl *wlog.WL\n   514→\t\twblDir := filepath.Join(db.dir, wlog.WblDirName)\n   515→\t\tif _, err := os.Stat(wblDir); !os.IsNotExist(err) {\n   516→\t\t\twbl, err = wlog.Open(db.logger, wblDir)\n   517→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   518→\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   519→\t\t\t}\n   520→\t\t}\n   521→\t\topts := DefaultHeadOptions()\n   522→\t\topts.ChunkDirRoot = db.dir\n   523→\t\thead, err = NewHead(nil, db.logger, w, wbl, opts, NewHeadStats())\n   524→\t\tif err != nil {\n   525→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   526→\t\t}\n   527→\t\t// Set the min valid time for the ingested wal samples\n   528→\t\t// to be no lower than the maxt of the last block.\n   529→\t\tif err := head.Init(maxBlockTime); err != nil {\n   530→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"read WAL: %w\", err)\n   531→\t\t}\n   532→\t\t// Set the wal and the wbl to nil to disable related operations.\n   533→\t\t// This is mainly to avoid blocking when closing the head.\n   534→\t\thead.wal = nil\n   535→\t\thead.wbl = nil\n   536→\t}\n   537→\n   538→\tdb.closers = append(db.closers, head)\n   539→\treturn &DB{\n   540→\t\tdir:    db.dir,\n   541→\t\tlogger: db.logger,\n   542→\t\tblocks: blocks,\n   543→\t\thead:   head,\n   544→\t}, nil\n   545→}\n   546→\n   547→// Querier loads the blocks and wal and returns a new querier over the data partition for the given time range.\n   548→// Current implementation doesn't support multiple Queriers.\n   549→func (db *DBReadOnly) Querier(mint, maxt int64) (storage.Querier, error) {\n   550→\tq, err := db.loadDataAsQueryable(maxt)\n   551→\tif err != nil {\n   552→\t\treturn nil, err\n   553→\t}\n   554→\treturn q.Querier(mint, maxt)\n   555→}\n   556→\n   557→// ChunkQuerier loads blocks and the wal and returns a new chunk querier over the data partition for the given time range.\n   558→// Current implementation doesn't support multiple ChunkQueriers.\n   559→func (db *DBReadOnly) ChunkQuerier(mint, maxt int64) (storage.ChunkQuerier, error) {\n   560→\tq, err := db.loadDataAsQueryable(maxt)\n   561→\tif err != nil {\n   562→\t\treturn nil, err\n   563→\t}\n   564→\treturn q.ChunkQuerier(mint, maxt)\n   565→}\n   566→\n   567→// Blocks returns a slice of block readers for persisted blocks.\n   568→func (db *DBReadOnly) Blocks() ([]BlockReader, error) {\n   569→\tselect {\n   570→\tcase <-db.closed:\n   571→\t\treturn nil, ErrClosed\n   572→\tdefault:\n   573→\t}\n   574→\tloadable, corrupted, err := openBlocks(db.logger, db.dir, nil, nil)\n   575→\tif err != nil {\n   576→\t\treturn nil, err\n   577→\t}\n   578→\n   579→\t// Corrupted blocks that have been superseded by a loadable block can be safely ignored.\n   580→\tfor _, block := range loadable {\n   581→\t\tfor _, b := range block.Meta().Compaction.Parents {\n   582→\t\t\tdelete(corrupted, b.ULID)\n   583→\t\t}\n   584→\t}\n   585→\tif len(corrupted) > 0 {\n   586→\t\tfor _, b := range loadable {\n   587→\t\t\tif err := b.Close(); err != nil {\n   588→\t\t\t\tlevel.Warn(db.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"Closing block failed\", \"err\", err, \"block\", b)\n   589→\t\t\t}\n   590→\t\t}\n   591→\t\terrs := tsdb_errors.NewMulti()\n   592→\t\tfor ulid, err := range corrupted {\n   593→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   594→\t\t\t\terrs.Add(fmt.Errorf(\"corrupted block %s: %w\", ulid.String(), err))\n   595→\t\t\t}\n   596→\t\t}\n   597→\t\treturn nil, errs.Err()\n   598→\t}\n   599→\n   600→\tif len(loadable) == 0 {\n   601→\t\treturn nil, nil\n   602→\t}\n   603→\n   604→\tslices.SortFunc(loadable, func(a, b *Block) int {\n   605→\t\tswitch {\n   606→\t\tcase a.Meta().MinTime < b.Meta().MinTime:\n   607→\t\t\treturn -1\n   608→\t\tcase a.Meta().MinTime > b.Meta().MinTime:\n   609→\t\t\treturn 1\n   610→\t\tdefault:\n   611→\t\t\treturn 0\n   612→\t\t}\n   613→\t})\n   614→\n   615→\tblockMetas := make([]BlockMeta, 0, len(loadable))\n   616→\tfor _, b := range loadable {\n   617→\t\tblockMetas = append(blockMetas, b.Meta())\n   618→\t}\n   619→\tif overlaps := OverlappingBlocks(blockMetas); len(overlaps) > 0 {\n   620→\t\tlevel.Warn(db.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"Overlapping blocks found during opening\", \"detail\", overlaps.String())\n   621→\t}\n   622→\n   623→\t// Close all previously open readers and add the new ones to the cache.\n   624→\tfor _, closer := range db.closers {\n   625→\t\tcloser.Close()\n   626→\t}\n   627→\n   628→\tblockClosers := make([]io.Closer, len(loadable))\n   629→\tblockReaders := make([]BlockReader, len(loadable))\n   630→\tfor i, b := range loadable {\n   631→\t\tblockClosers[i] = b\n   632→\t\tblockReaders[i] = b\n   633→\t}\n   634→\tdb.closers = blockClosers\n   635→\n   636→\treturn blockReaders, nil\n   637→}\n   638→\n   639→// LastBlockID returns the BlockID of latest block.\n   640→func (db *DBReadOnly) LastBlockID() (string, error) {\n   641→\tentries, err := os.ReadDir(db.dir)\n   642→\tif err != nil {\n   643→\t\treturn \"\", err\n   644→\t}\n   645→\n   646→\tmax := uint64(0)\n   647→\n   648→\tlastBlockID := \"\"\n   649→\n   650→\tfor _, e := range entries {\n   651→\t\t// Check if dir is a block dir or not.\n   652→\t\tdirName := e.Name()\n   653→\t\tulidObj, err := ulid.ParseStrict(dirName)\n   654→\t\tif err != nil {\n   655→\t\t\tcontinue // Not a block dir.\n   656→\t\t}\n   657→\t\ttimestamp := ulidObj.Time()\n   658→\t\tif timestamp > max {\n   659→\t\t\tmax = timestamp\n   660→\t\t\tlastBlockID = dirName\n   661→\t\t}\n   662→\t}\n   663→\n   664→\tif lastBlockID == \"\" {\n   665→\t\treturn \"\", errors.New(\"no blocks found\")\n   666→\t}\n   667→\n   668→\treturn lastBlockID, nil\n   669→}\n   670→\n   671→// Block returns a block reader by given block id.\n   672→func (db *DBReadOnly) Block(blockID string) (BlockReader, error) {\n   673→\tselect {\n   674→\tcase <-db.closed:\n   675→\t\treturn nil, ErrClosed\n   676→\tdefault:\n   677→\t}\n   678→\n   679→\t_, err := os.Stat(filepath.Join(db.dir, blockID))\n   680→\tif os.IsNotExist(err) {\n   681→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"invalid block ID %s\", blockID)\n   682→\t}\n   683→\n   684→\tblock, err := OpenBlock(db.logger, filepath.Join(db.dir, blockID), nil)\n   685→\tif err != nil {\n   686→\t\treturn nil, err\n   687→\t}\n   688→\tdb.closers = append(db.closers, block)\n   689→\n   690→\treturn block, nil\n   691→}\n   692→\n   693→// Close all block readers.\n   694→func (db *DBReadOnly) Close() error {\n   695→\tselect {\n   696→\tcase <-db.closed:\n   697→\t\treturn ErrClosed\n   698→\tdefault:\n   699→\t}\n   700→\tclose(db.closed)\n   701→\n   702→\treturn tsdb_errors.CloseAll(db.closers)\n   703→}\n   704→\n   705→// Open returns a new DB in the given directory. If options are empty, DefaultOptions will be used.\n   706→func Open(dir string, l log.Logger, r prometheus.Registerer, opts *Options, stats *DBStats) (db *DB, err error) {\n   707→\tvar rngs []int64\n   708→\topts, rngs = validateOpts(opts, nil)\n   709→\n   710→\treturn open(dir, l, r, opts, rngs, stats)\n   711→}\n   712→\n   713→func validateOpts(opts *Options, rngs []int64) (*Options, []int64) {\n   714→\tif opts == nil {\n   715→\t\topts = DefaultOptions()\n   716→\t}\n   717→\tif opts.StripeSize <= 0 {\n   718→\t\topts.StripeSize = DefaultStripeSize\n   719→\t}\n   720→\tif opts.HeadChunksWriteBufferSize <= 0 {\n   721→\t\topts.HeadChunksWriteBufferSize = chunks.DefaultWriteBufferSize\n   722→\t}\n   723→\tif opts.HeadChunksWriteQueueSize < 0 {\n   724→\t\topts.HeadChunksWriteQueueSize = chunks.DefaultWriteQueueSize\n   725→\t}\n   726→\tif opts.SamplesPerChunk <= 0 {\n   727→\t\topts.SamplesPerChunk = DefaultSamplesPerChunk\n   728→\t}\n   729→\tif opts.MaxBlockChunkSegmentSize <= 0 {\n   730→\t\topts.MaxBlockChunkSegmentSize = chunks.DefaultChunkSegmentSize\n   731→\t}\n   732→\tif opts.MinBlockDuration <= 0 {\n   733→\t\topts.MinBlockDuration = DefaultBlockDuration\n   734→\t}\n   735→\tif opts.MinBlockDuration > opts.MaxBlockDuration {\n   736→\t\topts.MaxBlockDuration = opts.MinBlockDuration\n   737→\t}\n   738→\tif opts.OutOfOrderCapMax <= 0 {\n   739→\t\topts.OutOfOrderCapMax = DefaultOutOfOrderCapMax\n   740→\t}\n   741→\tif opts.OutOfOrderTimeWindow < 0 {\n   742→\t\topts.OutOfOrderTimeWindow = 0\n   743→\t}\n   744→\n   745→\tif len(rngs) == 0 {\n   746→\t\t// Start with smallest block duration and create exponential buckets until the exceed the\n   747→\t\t// configured maximum block duration.\n   748→\t\trngs = ExponentialBlockRanges(opts.MinBlockDuration, 10, 3)\n   749→\t}\n   750→\treturn opts, rngs\n   751→}\n   752→\n   753→// open returns a new DB in the given directory.\n   754→// It initializes the lockfile, WAL, compactor, and Head (by replaying the WAL), and runs the database.\n   755→// It is not safe to open more than one DB in the same directory.\n   756→func open(dir string, l log.Logger, r prometheus.Registerer, opts *Options, rngs []int64, stats *DBStats) (_ *DB, returnedErr error) {\n   757→\tif err := os.MkdirAll(dir, 0o777); err != nil {\n   758→\t\treturn nil, err\n   759→\t}\n   760→\tif l == nil {\n   761→\t\tl = log.NewNopLogger()\n   762→\t}\n   763→\tif stats == nil {\n   764→\t\tstats = NewDBStats()\n   765→\t}\n   766→\n   767→\tfor i, v := range rngs {\n   768→\t\tif v > opts.MaxBlockDuration {\n   769→\t\t\trngs = rngs[:i]\n   770→\t\t\tbreak\n   771→\t\t}\n   772→\t}\n   773→\n   774→\t// Fixup bad format written by Prometheus 2.1.\n   775→\tif err := repairBadIndexVersion(l, dir); err != nil {\n   776→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"repair bad index version: %w\", err)\n   777→\t}\n   778→\n   779→\twalDir := filepath.Join(dir, \"wal\")\n   780→\twblDir := filepath.Join(dir, wlog.WblDirName)\n   781→\n   782→\tfor _, tmpDir := range []string{walDir, dir} {\n   783→\t\t// Remove tmp dirs.\n   784→\t\tif err := removeBestEffortTmpDirs(l, tmpDir); err != nil {\n   785→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"remove tmp dirs: %w\", err)\n   786→\t\t}\n   787→\t}\n   788→\n   789→\tdb := &DB{\n   790→\t\tdir:            dir,\n   791→\t\tlogger:         l,\n   792→\t\topts:           opts,\n   793→\t\tcompactc:       make(chan struct{}, 1),\n   794→\t\tdonec:          make(chan struct{}),\n   795→\t\tstopc:          make(chan struct{}),\n   796→\t\tautoCompact:    true,\n   797→\t\tchunkPool:      chunkenc.NewPool(),\n   798→\t\tblocksToDelete: opts.BlocksToDelete,\n   799→\t\tregisterer:     r,\n   800→\t}\n   801→\tdefer func() {\n   802→\t\t// Close files if startup fails somewhere.\n   803→\t\tif returnedErr == nil {\n   804→\t\t\treturn\n   805→\t\t}\n   806→\n   807→\t\tclose(db.donec) // DB is never run if it was an error, so close this channel here.\n   808→\t\terrs := tsdb_errors.NewMulti(returnedErr)\n   809→\t\tif err := db.Close(); err != nil {\n   810→\t\t\terrs.Add(fmt.Errorf(\"close DB after failed startup: %w\", err))\n   811→\t\t}\n   812→\t\treturnedErr = errs.Err()\n   813→\t}()\n   814→\n   815→\tif db.blocksToDelete == nil {\n   816→\t\tdb.blocksToDelete = DefaultBlocksToDelete(db)\n   817→\t}\n   818→\n   819→\tvar err error\n   820→\tdb.locker, err = tsdbutil.NewDirLocker(dir, \"tsdb\", db.logger, r)\n   821→\tif err != nil {\n   822→\t\treturn nil, err\n   823→\t}\n   824→\tif !opts.NoLockfile {\n   825→\t\tif err := db.locker.Lock(); err != nil {\n   826→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   827→\t\t}\n   828→\t}\n   829→\n   830→\tctx, cancel := context.WithCancel(context.Background())\n   831→\tdb.compactor, err = NewLeveledCompactorWithOptions(ctx, r, l, rngs, db.chunkPool, LeveledCompactorOptions{\n   832→\t\tMaxBlockChunkSegmentSize:    opts.MaxBlockChunkSegmentSize,\n   833→\t\tEnableOverlappingCompaction: opts.EnableOverlappingCompaction,\n   834→\t})\n   835→\tif err != nil {\n   836→\t\tcancel()\n   837→\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"create leveled compactor: %w\", err)\n   838→\t}\n   839→\tdb.compactCancel = cancel\n   840→\n   841→\tvar wal, wbl *wlog.WL\n   842→\tsegmentSize := wlog.DefaultSegmentSize\n   843→\t// Wal is enabled.\n   844→\tif opts.WALSegmentSize >= 0 {\n   845→\t\t// Wal is set to a custom size.\n   846→\t\tif opts.WALSegmentSize > 0 {\n   847→\t\t\tsegmentSize = opts.WALSegmentSize\n   848→\t\t}\n   849→\t\twal, err = wlog.NewSize(l, r, walDir, segmentSize, opts.WALCompression)\n   850→\t\tif err != nil {\n   851→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   852→\t\t}\n   853→\t\t// Check if there is a WBL on disk, in which case we should replay that data.\n   854→\t\twblSize, err := fileutil.DirSize(wblDir)\n   855→\t\tif err != nil && !os.IsNotExist(err) {\n   856→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   857→\t\t}\n   858→\t\tif opts.OutOfOrderTimeWindow > 0 || wblSize > 0 {\n   859→\t\t\twbl, err = wlog.NewSize(l, r, wblDir, segmentSize, opts.WALCompression)\n   860→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n   861→\t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n   862→\t\t\t}\n   863→\t\t}\n   864→\t}\n   865→\tdb.oooWasEnabled.Store(opts.OutOfOrderTimeWindow > 0)\n   866→\theadOpts := DefaultHeadOptions()\n   867→\theadOpts.ChunkRange = rngs[0]\n   868→\theadOpts.ChunkDirRoot = dir\n   869→\theadOpts.ChunkPool = db.chunkPool\n   870→\theadOpts.ChunkWriteBufferSize = opts.HeadChunksWriteBufferSize\n   871→\theadOpts.ChunkWriteQueueSize = opts.HeadChunksWriteQueueSize\n   872→\theadOpts.SamplesPerChunk = opts.SamplesPerChunk\n   873→\theadOpts.StripeSize = opts.StripeSize\n   874→\theadOpts.SeriesCallback = opts.SeriesLifecycleCallback\n   875→\theadOpts.EnableExemplarStorage = opts.EnableExemplarStorage\n   876→\theadOpts.MaxExemplars.Store(opts.MaxExemplars)\n   877→\theadOpts.EnableMemorySnapshotOnShutdown = opts.EnableMemorySnapshotOnShutdown\n   878→\theadOpts.EnableNativeHistograms.Store(opts.EnableNativeHistograms)\n   879→\theadOpts.OutOfOrderTimeWindow.Store(opts.OutOfOrderTimeWindow)\n   880→\theadOpts.OutOfOrderCapMax.Store(opts.OutOfOrderCapMax)\n   881→\theadOpts.EnableSharding = opts.EnableSharding\n   882→\tif opts.WALReplayConcurrency > 0 {\n   883→\t\theadOpts.WALReplayConcurrency = opts.WALReplayConcurrency\n   884→\t}\n   885→\tif opts.IsolationDisabled {\n   886→\t\t// We only override this flag if isolation is disabled at DB level. We use the default otherwise.\n   887→\t\theadOpts.IsolationDisabled = opts.IsolationDisabled\n   888→\t}\n   889→\tdb.head, err = NewHead(r, l, wal, wbl, headOpts, stats.Head)\n   890→\tif err != nil {\n   891→\t\treturn nil, err\n   892→\t}\n   893→\tdb.head.writeNotified = db.writeNotified\n   894→\n   895→\t// Register metrics after assigning the head block.\n   896→\tdb.metrics = newDBMetrics(db, r)\n   897→\tmaxBytes := opts.MaxBytes\n   898→\tif maxBytes < 0 {\n   899→\t\tmaxBytes = 0\n   900→\t}\n   901→\tdb.metrics.maxBytes.Set(float64(maxBytes))\n   902→\tdb.metrics.retentionDuration.Set((time.Duration(opts.RetentionDuration) * time.Millisecond).Seconds())\n   903→\n   904→\tif err := db.reload(); err != nil {\n   905→\t\treturn nil, err\n   906→\t}\n   907→\t// Set the min valid time for the ingested samples\n   908→\t// to be no lower than the maxt of the last block.\n   909→\tminValidTime := int64(math.MinInt64)\n   910→\t// We do not consider blocks created from out-of-order samples for Head's minValidTime\n   911→\t// since minValidTime is only for the in-order data and we do not want to discard unnecessary\n   912→\t// samples from the Head.\n   913→\tinOrderMaxTime, ok := db.inOrderBlocksMaxTime()\n   914→\tif ok {\n   915→\t\tminValidTime = inOrderMaxTime\n   916→\t}\n   917→\n   918→\tif initErr := db.head.Init(minValidTime); initErr != nil {\n   919→\t\tdb.head.metrics.walCorruptionsTotal.Inc()\n   920→\t\tvar e *errLoadWbl\n   921→\t\tif errors.As(initErr, &e) {\n   922→\t\t\tlevel.Warn(db.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"Encountered WBL read error, attempting repair\", \"err\", initErr)\n   923→\t\t\tif err := wbl.Repair(e.err); err != nil {\n   924→\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"repair corrupted WBL: %w\", err)\n   925→\t\t\t}\n   926→\t\t\tlevel.Info(db.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"Successfully repaired WBL\")\n   927→\t\t} else {\n   928→\t\t\tlevel.Warn(db.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"Encountered WAL read error, attempting repair\", \"err\", initErr)\n   929→\t\t\tif err := wal.Repair(initErr); err != nil {\n   930→\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"repair corrupted WAL: %w\", err)\n   931→\t\t\t}\n   932→\t\t\tlevel.Info(db.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"Successfully repaired WAL\")\n   933→\t\t}\n   934→\t}\n   935→\n   936→\tif db.head.MinOOOTime() != int64(math.MaxInt64) {\n   937→\t\t// Some OOO data was replayed from the disk that needs compaction and cleanup.\n   938→\t\tdb.oooWasEnabled.Store(true)\n   939→\t}\n   940→\n   941→\tgo db.run(ctx)\n   942→\n   943→\treturn db, nil\n   944→}\n   945→\n   946→func removeBestEffortTmpDirs(l log.Logger, dir string) error {\n   947→\tfiles, err := os.ReadDir(dir)\n   948→\tif os.IsNotExist(err) {\n   949→\t\treturn nil\n   950→\t}\n   951→\tif err != nil {\n   952→\t\treturn err\n   953→\t}\n   954→\tfor _, f := range files {\n   955→\t\tif isTmpDir(f) {\n   956→\t\t\tif err := os.RemoveAll(filepath.Join(dir, f.Name())); err != nil {\n   957→\t\t\t\tlevel.Error(l).Log(\"msg\", \"failed to delete tmp block dir\", \"dir\", filepath.Join(dir, f.Name()), \"err\", err)\n   958→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n   959→\t\t\t}\n   960→\t\t\tlevel.Info(l).Log(\"msg\", \"Found and deleted tmp block dir\", \"dir\", filepath.Join(dir, f.Name()))\n   961→\t\t}\n   962→\t}\n   963→\treturn nil\n   964→}\n   965→\n   966→// StartTime implements the Storage interface.\n   967→func (db *DB) StartTime() (int64, error) {\n   968→\tdb.mtx.RLock()\n   969→\tdefer db.mtx.RUnlock()\n   970→\n   971→\tif len(db.blocks) > 0 {\n   972→\t\treturn db.blocks[0].Meta().MinTime, nil\n   973→\t}\n   974→\treturn db.head.MinTime(), nil\n   975→}\n   976→\n   977→// Dir returns the directory of the database.\n   978→func (db *DB) Dir() string {\n   979→\treturn db.dir\n   980→}\n   981→\n   982→func (db *DB) run(ctx context.Context) {\n   983→\tdefer close(db.donec)\n   984→\n   985→\tbackoff := time.Duration(0)\n   986→\n   987→\tfor {\n   988→\t\tselect {\n   989→\t\tcase <-db.stopc:\n   990→\t\t\treturn\n   991→\t\tcase <-time.After(backoff):\n   992→\t\t}\n   993→\n   994→\t\tselect {\n   995→\t\tcase <-time.After(1 * time.Minute):\n   996→\t\t\tdb.cmtx.Lock()\n   997→\t\t\tif err := db.reloadBlocks(); err != nil {\n   998→\t\t\t\tlevel.Error(db.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"reloadBlocks\", \"err\", err)\n   999→\t\t\t}\n  1000→\t\t\tdb.cmtx.Unlock()\n  1001→\n  1002→\t\t\tselect {\n  1003→\t\t\tcase db.compactc <- struct{}{}:\n  1004→\t\t\tdefault:\n  1005→\t\t\t}\n  1006→\t\t\t// We attempt mmapping of head chunks regularly.\n  1007→\t\t\tdb.head.mmapHeadChunks()\n  1008→\t\tcase <-db.compactc:\n  1009→\t\t\tdb.metrics.compactionsTriggered.Inc()\n  1010→\n  1011→\t\t\tdb.autoCompactMtx.Lock()\n  1012→\t\t\tif db.autoCompact {\n  1013→\t\t\t\tif err := db.Compact(ctx); err != nil {\n  1014→\t\t\t\t\tlevel.Error(db.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"compaction failed\", \"err\", err)\n  1015→\t\t\t\t\tbackoff = exponential(backoff, 1*time.Second, 1*time.Minute)\n  1016→\t\t\t\t} else {\n  1017→\t\t\t\t\tbackoff = 0\n  1018→\t\t\t\t}\n  1019→\t\t\t} else {\n  1020→\t\t\t\tdb.metrics.compactionsSkipped.Inc()\n  1021→\t\t\t}\n  1022→\t\t\tdb.autoCompactMtx.Unlock()\n  1023→\t\tcase <-db.stopc:\n  1024→\t\t\treturn\n  1025→\t\t}\n  1026→\t}\n  1027→}\n  1028→\n  1029→// Appender opens a new appender against the database.\n  1030→func (db *DB) Appender(ctx context.Context) storage.Appender {\n  1031→\treturn dbAppender{db: db, Appender: db.head.Appender(ctx)}\n  1032→}\n  1033→\n  1034→// ApplyConfig applies a new config to the DB.\n  1035→// Behaviour of 'OutOfOrderTimeWindow' is as follows:\n  1036→// OOO enabled = oooTimeWindow > 0. OOO disabled = oooTimeWindow is 0.\n  1037→// 1) Before: OOO disabled, Now: OOO enabled =>\n  1038→//   - A new WBL is created for the head block.\n  1039→//   - OOO compaction is enabled.\n  1040→//   - Overlapping queries are enabled.\n  1041→//\n  1042→// 2) Before: OOO enabled, Now: OOO enabled =>\n  1043→//   - Only the time window is updated.\n  1044→//\n  1045→// 3) Before: OOO enabled, Now: OOO disabled =>\n  1046→//   - Time Window set to 0. So no new OOO samples will be allowed.\n  1047→//   - OOO WBL will stay and will be eventually cleaned up.\n  1048→//   - OOO Compaction and overlapping queries will remain enabled until a restart or until all OOO samples are compacted.\n  1049→//\n  1050→// 4) Before: OOO disabled, Now: OOO disabled => no-op.\n  1051→func (db *DB) ApplyConfig(conf *config.Config) error {\n  1052→\toooTimeWindow := int64(0)\n  1053→\tif conf.StorageConfig.TSDBConfig != nil {\n  1054→\t\toooTimeWindow = conf.StorageConfig.TSDBConfig.OutOfOrderTimeWindow\n  1055→\t}\n  1056→\tif oooTimeWindow < 0 {\n  1057→\t\toooTimeWindow = 0\n  1058→\t}\n  1059→\n  1060→\t// Create WBL if it was not present and if OOO is enabled with WAL enabled.\n  1061→\tvar wblog *wlog.WL\n  1062→\tvar err error\n  1063→\tswitch {\n  1064→\tcase db.head.wbl != nil:\n  1065→\t\t// The existing WBL from the disk might have been replayed while OOO was disabled.\n  1066→\t\twblog = db.head.wbl\n  1067→\tcase !db.oooWasEnabled.Load() && oooTimeWindow > 0 && db.opts.WALSegmentSize >= 0:\n  1068→\t\tsegmentSize := wlog.DefaultSegmentSize\n  1069→\t\t// Wal is set to a custom size.\n  1070→\t\tif db.opts.WALSegmentSize > 0 {\n  1071→\t\t\tsegmentSize = db.opts.WALSegmentSize\n  1072→\t\t}\n  1073→\t\toooWalDir := filepath.Join(db.dir, wlog.WblDirName)\n  1074→\t\twblog, err = wlog.NewSize(db.logger, db.registerer, oooWalDir, segmentSize, db.opts.WALCompression)\n  1075→\t\tif err != nil {\n  1076→\t\t\treturn err\n  1077→\t\t}\n  1078→\t}\n  1079→\n  1080→\tdb.opts.OutOfOrderTimeWindow = oooTimeWindow\n  1081→\tdb.head.ApplyConfig(conf, wblog)\n  1082→\n  1083→\tif !db.oooWasEnabled.Load() {\n  1084→\t\tdb.oooWasEnabled.Store(oooTimeWindow > 0)\n  1085→\t}\n  1086→\treturn nil\n  1087→}\n  1088→\n  1089→// EnableNativeHistograms enables the native histogram feature.\n  1090→func (db *DB) EnableNativeHistograms() {\n  1091→\tdb.head.EnableNativeHistograms()\n  1092→}\n  1093→\n  1094→// DisableNativeHistograms disables the native histogram feature.\n  1095→func (db *DB) DisableNativeHistograms() {\n  1096→\tdb.head.DisableNativeHistograms()\n  1097→}\n  1098→\n  1099→// dbAppender wraps the DB's head appender and triggers compactions on commit\n  1100→// if necessary.\n  1101→type dbAppender struct {\n  1102→\tstorage.Appender\n  1103→\tdb *DB\n  1104→}\n  1105→\n  1106→var _ storage.GetRef = dbAppender{}\n  1107→\n  1108→func (a dbAppender) GetRef(lset labels.Labels, hash uint64) (storage.SeriesRef, labels.Labels) {\n  1109→\tif g, ok := a.Appender.(storage.GetRef); ok {\n  1110→\t\treturn g.GetRef(lset, hash)\n  1111→\t}\n  1112→\treturn 0, labels.EmptyLabels()\n  1113→}\n  1114→\n  1115→func (a dbAppender) Commit() error {\n  1116→\terr := a.Appender.Commit()\n  1117→\n  1118→\t// We could just run this check every few minutes practically. But for benchmarks\n  1119→\t// and high frequency use cases this is the safer way.\n  1120→\tif a.db.head.compactable() {\n  1121→\t\tselect {\n  1122→\t\tcase a.db.compactc <- struct{}{}:\n  1123→\t\tdefault:\n  1124→\t\t}\n  1125→\t}\n  1126→\treturn err\n  1127→}\n  1128→\n  1129→// Compact data if possible. After successful compaction blocks are reloaded\n  1130→// which will also delete the blocks that fall out of the retention window.\n  1131→// Old blocks are only deleted on reloadBlocks based on the new block's parent information.\n  1132→// See DB.reloadBlocks documentation for further information.\n  1133→func (db *DB) Compact(ctx context.Context) (returnErr error) {\n  1134→\tdb.cmtx.Lock()\n  1135→\tdefer db.cmtx.Unlock()\n  1136→\tdefer func() {\n  1137→\t\tif returnErr != nil && !errors.Is(returnErr, context.Canceled) {\n  1138→\t\t\t// If we got an error because context was canceled then we're most likely\n  1139→\t\t\t// shutting down TSDB and we don't need to report this on metrics\n  1140→\t\t\tdb.metrics.compactionsFailed.Inc()\n  1141→\t\t}\n  1142→\t}()\n  1143→\n  1144→\tlastBlockMaxt := int64(math.MinInt64)\n  1145→\tdefer func() {\n  1146→\t\terrs := tsdb_errors.NewMulti(returnErr)\n  1147→\t\tif err := db.head.truncateWAL(lastBlockMaxt); err != nil {\n  1148→\t\t\terrs.Add(fmt.Errorf(\"WAL truncation in Compact defer: %w\", err))\n  1149→\t\t}\n  1150→\t\treturnErr = errs.Err()\n  1151→\t}()\n  1152→\n  1153→\tstart := time.Now()\n  1154→\t// Check whether we have pending head blocks that are ready to be persisted.\n  1155→\t// They have the highest priority.\n  1156→\tfor {\n  1157→\t\tselect {\n  1158→\t\tcase <-db.stopc:\n  1159→\t\t\treturn nil\n  1160→\t\tdefault:\n  1161→\t\t}\n  1162→\t\tif !db.head.compactable() {\n  1163→\t\t\tbreak\n  1164→\t\t}\n  1165→\t\tmint := db.head.MinTime()\n  1166→\t\tmaxt := rangeForTimestamp(mint, db.head.chunkRange.Load())\n  1167→\n  1168→\t\t// Wrap head into a range that bounds all reads to it.\n  1169→\t\t// We remove 1 millisecond from maxt because block\n  1170→\t\t// intervals are half-open: [b.MinTime, b.MaxTime). But\n  1171→\t\t// chunk intervals are closed: [c.MinTime, c.MaxTime];\n  1172→\t\t// so in order to make sure that overlaps are evaluated\n  1173→\t\t// consistently, we explicitly remove the last value\n  1174→\t\t// from the block interval here.\n  1175→\t\trh := NewRangeHeadWithIsolationDisabled(db.head, mint, maxt-1)\n  1176→\n  1177→\t\t// Compaction runs with isolation disabled, because head.compactable()\n  1178→\t\t// ensures that maxt is more than chunkRange/2 back from now, and\n  1179→\t\t// head.appendableMinValidTime() ensures that no new appends can start within the compaction range.\n  1180→\t\t// We do need to wait for any overlapping appenders that started previously to finish.\n  1181→\t\tdb.head.WaitForAppendersOverlapping(rh.MaxTime())\n  1182→\n  1183→\t\tif err := db.compactHead(rh); err != nil {\n  1184→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"compact head: %w\", err)\n  1185→\t\t}\n  1186→\t\t// Consider only successful compactions for WAL truncation.\n  1187→\t\tlastBlockMaxt = maxt\n  1188→\t}\n  1189→\n  1190→\t// Clear some disk space before compacting blocks, especially important\n  1191→\t// when Head compaction happened over a long time range.\n  1192→\tif err := db.head.truncateWAL(lastBlockMaxt); err != nil {\n  1193→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"WAL truncation in Compact: %w\", err)\n  1194→\t}\n  1195→\n  1196→\tcompactionDuration := time.Since(start)\n  1197→\tif compactionDuration.Milliseconds() > db.head.chunkRange.Load() {\n  1198→\t\tlevel.Warn(db.logger).Log(\n  1199→\t\t\t\"msg\", \"Head compaction took longer than the block time range, compactions are falling behind and won't be able to catch up\",\n  1200→\t\t\t\"duration\", compactionDuration.String(),\n  1201→\t\t\t\"block_range\", db.head.chunkRange.Load(),\n  1202→\t\t)\n  1203→\t}\n  1204→\n  1205→\tif lastBlockMaxt != math.MinInt64 {\n  1206→\t\t// The head was compacted, so we compact OOO head as well.\n  1207→\t\tif err := db.compactOOOHead(ctx); err != nil {\n  1208→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"compact ooo head: %w\", err)\n  1209→\t\t}\n  1210→\t}\n  1211→\n  1212→\treturn db.compactBlocks()\n  1213→}\n  1214→\n  1215→// CompactHead compacts the given RangeHead.\n  1216→func (db *DB) CompactHead(head *RangeHead) error {\n  1217→\tdb.cmtx.Lock()\n  1218→\tdefer db.cmtx.Unlock()\n  1219→\n  1220→\tif err := db.compactHead(head); err != nil {\n  1221→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"compact head: %w\", err)\n  1222→\t}\n  1223→\n  1224→\tif err := db.head.truncateWAL(head.BlockMaxTime()); err != nil {\n  1225→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"WAL truncation: %w\", err)\n  1226→\t}\n  1227→\treturn nil\n  1228→}\n  1229→\n  1230→// CompactOOOHead compacts the OOO Head.\n  1231→func (db *DB) CompactOOOHead(ctx context.Context) error {\n  1232→\tdb.cmtx.Lock()\n  1233→\tdefer db.cmtx.Unlock()\n  1234→\n  1235→\treturn db.compactOOOHead(ctx)\n  1236→}\n  1237→\n  1238→func (db *DB) compactOOOHead(ctx context.Context) error {\n  1239→\tif !db.oooWasEnabled.Load() {\n  1240→\t\treturn nil\n  1241→\t}\n  1242→\toooHead, err := NewOOOCompactionHead(ctx, db.head)\n  1243→\tif err != nil {\n  1244→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"get ooo compaction head: %w\", err)\n  1245→\t}\n  1246→\n  1247→\tulids, err := db.compactOOO(db.dir, oooHead)\n  1248→\tif err != nil {\n  1249→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"compact ooo head: %w\", err)\n  1250→\t}\n  1251→\tif err := db.reloadBlocks(); err != nil {\n  1252→\t\terrs := tsdb_errors.NewMulti(err)\n  1253→\t\tfor _, uid := range ulids {\n  1254→\t\t\tif errRemoveAll := os.RemoveAll(filepath.Join(db.dir, uid.String())); errRemoveAll != nil {\n  1255→\t\t\t\terrs.Add(errRemoveAll)\n  1256→\t\t\t}\n  1257→\t\t}\n  1258→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"reloadBlocks blocks after failed compact ooo head: %w\", errs.Err())\n  1259→\t}\n  1260→\n  1261→\tlastWBLFile, minOOOMmapRef := oooHead.LastWBLFile(), oooHead.LastMmapRef()\n  1262→\tif lastWBLFile != 0 || minOOOMmapRef != 0 {\n  1263→\t\tif minOOOMmapRef != 0 {\n  1264→\t\t\t// Ensure that no more queriers are created that will reference chunks we're about to garbage collect.\n  1265→\t\t\t// truncateOOO waits for any existing queriers that reference chunks we're about to garbage collect to\n  1266→\t\t\t// complete before running garbage collection, so we don't need to do that here.\n  1267→\t\t\t//\n  1268→\t\t\t// We take mtx to ensure that Querier() and ChunkQuerier() don't miss blocks: without this, they could\n  1269→\t\t\t// capture the list of blocks before the call to reloadBlocks() above runs, but then capture\n  1270→\t\t\t// lastGarbageCollectedMmapRef after we update it here, and therefore not query either the blocks we've just\n  1271→\t\t\t// written or the head chunks those blocks were created from.\n  1272→\t\t\tdb.mtx.Lock()\n  1273→\t\t\tdb.lastGarbageCollectedMmapRef = minOOOMmapRef\n  1274→\t\t\tdb.mtx.Unlock()\n  1275→\t\t}\n  1276→\n  1277→\t\tif err := db.head.truncateOOO(lastWBLFile, minOOOMmapRef); err != nil {\n  1278→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"truncate ooo wbl: %w\", err)\n  1279→\t\t}\n  1280→\t}\n  1281→\n  1282→\treturn nil\n  1283→}\n  1284→\n  1285→// compactOOO creates a new block per possible block range in the compactor's directory from the OOO Head given.\n  1286→// Each ULID in the result corresponds to a block in a unique time range.\n  1287→func (db *DB) compactOOO(dest string, oooHead *OOOCompactionHead) (_ []ulid.ULID, err error) {\n  1288→\tstart := time.Now()\n  1289→\n  1290→\tblockSize := oooHead.ChunkRange()\n  1291→\toooHeadMint, oooHeadMaxt := oooHead.MinTime(), oooHead.MaxTime()\n  1292→\tulids := make([]ulid.ULID, 0)\n  1293→\tdefer func() {\n  1294→\t\tif err != nil {\n  1295→\t\t\t// Best effort removal of created block on any error.\n  1296→\t\t\tfor _, uid := range ulids {\n  1297→\t\t\t\t_ = os.RemoveAll(filepath.Join(db.dir, uid.String()))\n  1298→\t\t\t}\n  1299→\t\t}\n  1300→\t}()\n  1301→\n  1302→\tmeta := &BlockMeta{}\n  1303→\tmeta.Compaction.SetOutOfOrder()\n  1304→\tfor t := blockSize * (oooHeadMint / blockSize); t <= oooHeadMaxt; t += blockSize {\n  1305→\t\tmint, maxt := t, t+blockSize\n  1306→\t\t// Block intervals are half-open: [b.MinTime, b.MaxTime). Block intervals are always +1 than the total samples it includes.\n  1307→\t\tuid, err := db.compactor.Write(dest, oooHead.CloneForTimeRange(mint, maxt-1), mint, maxt, meta)\n  1308→\t\tif err != nil {\n  1309→\t\t\treturn nil, err\n  1310→\t\t}\n  1311→\t\tif uid.Compare(ulid.ULID{}) != 0 {\n  1312→\t\t\tulids = append(ulids, uid)\n  1313→\t\t}\n  1314→\t}\n  1315→\n  1316→\tif len(ulids) == 0 {\n  1317→\t\tlevel.Info(db.logger).Log(\n  1318→\t\t\t\"msg\", \"compact ooo head resulted in no blocks\",\n  1319→\t\t\t\"duration\", time.Since(start),\n  1320→\t\t)\n  1321→\t\treturn nil, nil\n  1322→\t}\n  1323→\n  1324→\tlevel.Info(db.logger).Log(\n  1325→\t\t\"msg\", \"out-of-order compaction completed\",\n  1326→\t\t\"duration\", time.Since(start),\n  1327→\t\t\"ulids\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%v\", ulids),\n  1328→\t)\n  1329→\treturn ulids, nil\n  1330→}\n  1331→\n  1332→// compactHead compacts the given RangeHead.\n  1333→// The compaction mutex should be held before calling this method.\n  1334→func (db *DB) compactHead(head *RangeHead) error {\n  1335→\tuid, err := db.compactor.Write(db.dir, head, head.MinTime(), head.BlockMaxTime(), nil)\n  1336→\tif err != nil {\n  1337→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"persist head block: %w\", err)\n  1338→\t}\n  1339→\n  1340→\tif err := db.reloadBlocks(); err != nil {\n  1341→\t\tif errRemoveAll := os.RemoveAll(filepath.Join(db.dir, uid.String())); errRemoveAll != nil {\n  1342→\t\t\treturn tsdb_errors.NewMulti(\n  1343→\t\t\t\tfmt.Errorf(\"reloadBlocks blocks: %w\", err),\n  1344→\t\t\t\tfmt.Errorf(\"delete persisted head block after failed db reloadBlocks:%s: %w\", uid, errRemoveAll),\n  1345→\t\t\t).Err()\n  1346→\t\t}\n  1347→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"reloadBlocks blocks: %w\", err)\n  1348→\t}\n  1349→\tif err = db.head.truncateMemory(head.BlockMaxTime()); err != nil {\n  1350→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"head memory truncate: %w\", err)\n  1351→\t}\n  1352→\treturn nil\n  1353→}\n  1354→\n  1355→// compactBlocks compacts all the eligible on-disk blocks.\n  1356→// The compaction mutex should be held before calling this method.\n  1357→func (db *DB) compactBlocks() (err error) {\n  1358→\t// Check for compactions of multiple blocks.\n  1359→\tfor {\n  1360→\t\t// If we have a lot of blocks to compact the whole process might take\n  1361→\t\t// long enough that we end up with a HEAD block that needs to be written.\n  1362→\t\t// Check if that's the case and stop compactions early.\n  1363→\t\tif db.head.compactable() {\n  1364→\t\t\tlevel.Warn(db.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"aborting block compactions to persit the head block\")\n  1365→\t\t\treturn nil\n  1366→\t\t}\n  1367→\n  1368→\t\tplan, err := db.compactor.Plan(db.dir)\n  1369→\t\tif err != nil {\n  1370→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"plan compaction: %w\", err)\n  1371→\t\t}\n  1372→\t\tif len(plan) == 0 {\n  1373→\t\t\tbreak\n  1374→\t\t}\n  1375→\n  1376→\t\tselect {\n  1377→\t\tcase <-db.stopc:\n  1378→\t\t\treturn nil\n  1379→\t\tdefault:\n  1380→\t\t}\n  1381→\n  1382→\t\tuid, err := db.compactor.Compact(db.dir, plan, db.blocks)\n  1383→\t\tif err != nil {\n  1384→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"compact %s: %w\", plan, err)\n  1385→\t\t}\n  1386→\n  1387→\t\tif err := db.reloadBlocks(); err != nil {\n  1388→\t\t\tif err := os.RemoveAll(filepath.Join(db.dir, uid.String())); err != nil {\n  1389→\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"delete compacted block after failed db reloadBlocks:%s: %w\", uid, err)\n  1390→\t\t\t}\n  1391→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"reloadBlocks blocks: %w\", err)\n  1392→\t\t}\n  1393→\t}\n  1394→\n  1395→\treturn nil\n  1396→}\n  1397→\n  1398→// getBlock iterates a given block range to find a block by a given id.\n  1399→// If found it returns the block itself and a boolean to indicate that it was found.\n  1400→func getBlock(allBlocks []*Block, id ulid.ULID) (*Block, bool) {\n  1401→\tfor _, b := range allBlocks {\n  1402→\t\tif b.Meta().ULID == id {\n  1403→\t\t\treturn b, true\n  1404→\t\t}\n  1405→\t}\n  1406→\treturn nil, false\n  1407→}\n  1408→\n  1409→// reload reloads blocks and truncates the head and its WAL.\n  1410→func (db *DB) reload() error {\n  1411→\tif err := db.reloadBlocks(); err != nil {\n  1412→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"reloadBlocks: %w\", err)\n  1413→\t}\n  1414→\tmaxt, ok := db.inOrderBlocksMaxTime()\n  1415→\tif !ok {\n  1416→\t\treturn nil\n  1417→\t}\n  1418→\tif err := db.head.Truncate(maxt); err != nil {\n  1419→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"head truncate: %w\", err)\n  1420→\t}\n  1421→\treturn nil\n  1422→}\n  1423→\n  1424→// reloadBlocks reloads blocks without touching head.\n  1425→// Blocks that are obsolete due to replacement or retention will be deleted.\n  1426→func (db *DB) reloadBlocks() (err error) {\n  1427→\tdefer func() {\n  1428→\t\tif err != nil {\n  1429→\t\t\tdb.metrics.reloadsFailed.Inc()\n  1430→\t\t}\n  1431→\t\tdb.metrics.reloads.Inc()\n  1432→\t}()\n  1433→\n  1434→\t// Now that we reload TSDB every minute, there is high chance for race condition with a reload\n  1435→\t// triggered by CleanTombstones(). We need to lock the reload to avoid the situation where\n  1436→\t// a normal reload and CleanTombstones try to delete the same block.\n  1437→\tdb.mtx.Lock()\n  1438→\tdefer db.mtx.Unlock()\n  1439→\n  1440→\tloadable, corrupted, err := openBlocks(db.logger, db.dir, db.blocks, db.chunkPool)\n  1441→\tif err != nil {\n  1442→\t\treturn err\n  1443→\t}\n  1444→\n  1445→\tdeletableULIDs := db.blocksToDelete(loadable)\n  1446→\tdeletable := make(map[ulid.ULID]*Block, len(deletableULIDs))\n  1447→\n  1448→\t// Mark all parents of loaded blocks as deletable (no matter if they exists). This makes it resilient against the process\n  1449→\t// crashing towards the end of a compaction but before deletions. By doing that, we can pick up the deletion where it left off during a crash.\n  1450→\tfor _, block := range loadable {\n  1451→\t\tif _, ok := deletableULIDs[block.meta.ULID]; ok {\n  1452→\t\t\tdeletable[block.meta.ULID] = block\n  1453→\t\t}\n  1454→\t\tfor _, b := range block.Meta().Compaction.Parents {\n  1455→\t\t\tif _, ok := corrupted[b.ULID]; ok {\n  1456→\t\t\t\tdelete(corrupted, b.ULID)\n  1457→\t\t\t\tlevel.Warn(db.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"Found corrupted block, but replaced by compacted one so it's safe to delete. This should not happen with atomic deletes.\", \"block\", b.ULID)\n  1458→\t\t\t}\n  1459→\t\t\tdeletable[b.ULID] = nil\n  1460→\t\t}\n  1461→\t}\n  1462→\n  1463→\tif len(corrupted) > 0 {\n  1464→\t\t// Corrupted but no child loaded for it.\n  1465→\t\t// Close all new blocks to release the lock for windows.\n  1466→\t\tfor _, block := range loadable {\n  1467→\t\t\tif _, open := getBlock(db.blocks, block.Meta().ULID); !open {\n  1468→\t\t\t\tblock.Close()\n  1469→\t\t\t}\n  1470→\t\t}\n  1471→\t\terrs := tsdb_errors.NewMulti()\n  1472→\t\tfor ulid, err := range corrupted {\n  1473→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n  1474→\t\t\t\terrs.Add(fmt.Errorf(\"corrupted block %s: %w\", ulid.String(), err))\n  1475→\t\t\t}\n  1476→\t\t}\n  1477→\t\treturn errs.Err()\n  1478→\t}\n  1479→\n  1480→\tvar (\n  1481→\t\ttoLoad     []*Block\n  1482→\t\tblocksSize int64\n  1483→\t)\n  1484→\t// All deletable blocks should be unloaded.\n  1485→\t// NOTE: We need to loop through loadable one more time as there might be loadable ready to be removed (replaced by compacted block).\n  1486→\tfor _, block := range loadable {\n  1487→\t\tif _, ok := deletable[block.Meta().ULID]; ok {\n  1488→\t\t\tdeletable[block.Meta().ULID] = block\n  1489→\t\t\tcontinue\n  1490→\t\t}\n  1491→\n  1492→\t\ttoLoad = append(toLoad, block)\n  1493→\t\tblocksSize += block.Size()\n  1494→\t}\n  1495→\tdb.metrics.blocksBytes.Set(float64(blocksSize))\n  1496→\n  1497→\tslices.SortFunc(toLoad, func(a, b *Block) int {\n  1498→\t\tswitch {\n  1499→\t\tcase a.Meta().MinTime < b.Meta().MinTime:\n  1500→\t\t\treturn -1\n  1501→\t\tcase a.Meta().MinTime > b.Meta().MinTime:\n  1502→\t\t\treturn 1\n  1503→\t\tdefault:\n  1504→\t\t\treturn 0\n  1505→\t\t}\n  1506→\t})\n  1507→\n  1508→\t// Swap new blocks first for subsequently created readers to be seen.\n  1509→\toldBlocks := db.blocks\n  1510→\tdb.blocks = toLoad\n  1511→\n  1512→\tblockMetas := make([]BlockMeta, 0, len(toLoad))\n  1513→\tfor _, b := range toLoad {\n  1514→\t\tblockMetas = append(blockMetas, b.Meta())\n  1515→\t}\n  1516→\tif overlaps := OverlappingBlocks(blockMetas); len(overlaps) > 0 {\n  1517→\t\tlevel.Warn(db.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"Overlapping blocks found during reloadBlocks\", \"detail\", overlaps.String())\n  1518→\t}\n  1519→\n  1520→\t// Append blocks to old, deletable blocks, so we can close them.\n  1521→\tfor _, b := range oldBlocks {\n  1522→\t\tif _, ok := deletable[b.Meta().ULID]; ok {\n  1523→\t\t\tdeletable[b.Meta().ULID] = b\n  1524→\t\t}\n  1525→\t}\n  1526→\tif err := db.deleteBlocks(deletable); err != nil {\n  1527→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"delete %v blocks: %w\", len(deletable), err)\n  1528→\t}\n  1529→\treturn nil\n  1530→}\n  1531→\n  1532→func openBlocks(l log.Logger, dir string, loaded []*Block, chunkPool chunkenc.Pool) (blocks []*Block, corrupted map[ulid.ULID]error, err error) {\n  1533→\tbDirs, err := blockDirs(dir)\n  1534→\tif err != nil {\n  1535→\t\treturn nil, nil, fmt.Errorf(\"find blocks: %w\", err)\n  1536→\t}\n  1537→\n  1538→\tcorrupted = make(map[ulid.ULID]error)\n  1539→\tfor _, bDir := range bDirs {\n  1540→\t\tmeta, _, err := readMetaFile(bDir)\n  1541→\t\tif err != nil {\n  1542→\t\t\tlevel.Error(l).Log(\"msg\", \"Failed to read meta.json for a block during reloadBlocks. Skipping\", \"dir\", bDir, \"err\", err)\n  1543→\t\t\tcontinue\n  1544→\t\t}\n  1545→\n  1546→\t\t// See if we already have the block in memory or open it otherwise.\n  1547→\t\tblock, open := getBlock(loaded, meta.ULID)\n  1548→\t\tif !open {\n  1549→\t\t\tblock, err = OpenBlock(l, bDir, chunkPool)\n  1550→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n  1551→\t\t\t\tcorrupted[meta.ULID] = err\n  1552→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n  1553→\t\t\t}\n  1554→\t\t}\n  1555→\t\tblocks = append(blocks, block)\n  1556→\t}\n  1557→\treturn blocks, corrupted, nil\n  1558→}\n  1559→\n  1560→// DefaultBlocksToDelete returns a filter which decides time based and size based\n  1561→// retention from the options of the db.\n  1562→func DefaultBlocksToDelete(db *DB) BlocksToDeleteFunc {\n  1563→\treturn func(blocks []*Block) map[ulid.ULID]struct{} {\n  1564→\t\treturn deletableBlocks(db, blocks)\n  1565→\t}\n  1566→}\n  1567→\n  1568→// deletableBlocks returns all currently loaded blocks past retention policy or already compacted into a new block.\n  1569→func deletableBlocks(db *DB, blocks []*Block) map[ulid.ULID]struct{} {\n  1570→\tdeletable := make(map[ulid.ULID]struct{})\n  1571→\n  1572→\t// Sort the blocks by time - newest to oldest (largest to smallest timestamp).\n  1573→\t// This ensures that the retentions will remove the oldest  blocks.\n  1574→\tslices.SortFunc(blocks, func(a, b *Block) int {\n  1575→\t\tswitch {\n  1576→\t\tcase b.Meta().MaxTime < a.Meta().MaxTime:\n  1577→\t\t\treturn -1\n  1578→\t\tcase b.Meta().MaxTime > a.Meta().MaxTime:\n  1579→\t\t\treturn 1\n  1580→\t\tdefault:\n  1581→\t\t\treturn 0\n  1582→\t\t}\n  1583→\t})\n  1584→\n  1585→\tfor _, block := range blocks {\n  1586→\t\tif block.Meta().Compaction.Deletable {\n  1587→\t\t\tdeletable[block.Meta().ULID] = struct{}{}\n  1588→\t\t}\n  1589→\t}\n  1590→\n  1591→\tfor ulid := range BeyondTimeRetention(db, blocks) {\n  1592→\t\tdeletable[ulid] = struct{}{}\n  1593→\t}\n  1594→\n  1595→\tfor ulid := range BeyondSizeRetention(db, blocks) {\n  1596→\t\tdeletable[ulid] = struct{}{}\n  1597→\t}\n  1598→\n  1599→\treturn deletable\n  1600→}\n  1601→\n  1602→// BeyondTimeRetention returns those blocks which are beyond the time retention\n  1603→// set in the db options.\n  1604→func BeyondTimeRetention(db *DB, blocks []*Block) (deletable map[ulid.ULID]struct{}) {\n  1605→\t// Time retention is disabled or no blocks to work with.\n  1606→\tif len(blocks) == 0 || db.opts.RetentionDuration == 0 {\n  1607→\t\treturn\n  1608→\t}\n  1609→\n  1610→\tdeletable = make(map[ulid.ULID]struct{})\n  1611→\tfor i, block := range blocks {\n  1612→\t\t// The difference between the first block and this block is greater than or equal to\n  1613→\t\t// the retention period so any blocks after that are added as deletable.\n  1614→\t\tif i > 0 && blocks[0].Meta().MaxTime-block.Meta().MaxTime >= db.opts.RetentionDuration {\n  1615→\t\t\tfor _, b := range blocks[i:] {\n  1616→\t\t\t\tdeletable[b.meta.ULID] = struct{}{}\n  1617→\t\t\t}\n  1618→\t\t\tdb.metrics.timeRetentionCount.Inc()\n  1619→\t\t\tbreak\n  1620→\t\t}\n  1621→\t}\n  1622→\treturn deletable\n  1623→}\n  1624→\n  1625→// BeyondSizeRetention returns those blocks which are beyond the size retention\n  1626→// set in the db options.\n  1627→func BeyondSizeRetention(db *DB, blocks []*Block) (deletable map[ulid.ULID]struct{}) {\n  1628→\t// Size retention is disabled or no blocks to work with.\n  1629→\tif len(blocks) == 0 || db.opts.MaxBytes <= 0 {\n  1630→\t\treturn\n  1631→\t}\n  1632→\n  1633→\tdeletable = make(map[ulid.ULID]struct{})\n  1634→\n  1635→\t// Initializing size counter with WAL size and Head chunks\n  1636→\t// written to disk, as that is part of the retention strategy.\n  1637→\tblocksSize := db.Head().Size()\n  1638→\tfor i, block := range blocks {\n  1639→\t\tblocksSize += block.Size()\n  1640→\t\tif blocksSize > db.opts.MaxBytes {\n  1641→\t\t\t// Add this and all following blocks for deletion.\n  1642→\t\t\tfor _, b := range blocks[i:] {\n  1643→\t\t\t\tdeletable[b.meta.ULID] = struct{}{}\n  1644→\t\t\t}\n  1645→\t\t\tdb.metrics.sizeRetentionCount.Inc()\n  1646→\t\t\tbreak\n  1647→\t\t}\n  1648→\t}\n  1649→\treturn deletable\n  1650→}\n  1651→\n  1652→// deleteBlocks closes the block if loaded and deletes blocks from the disk if exists.\n  1653→// When the map contains a non nil block object it means it is loaded in memory\n  1654→// so needs to be closed first as it might need to wait for pending readers to complete.\n  1655→func (db *DB) deleteBlocks(blocks map[ulid.ULID]*Block) error {\n  1656→\tfor ulid, block := range blocks {\n  1657→\t\tif block != nil {\n  1658→\t\t\tif err := block.Close(); err != nil {\n  1659→\t\t\t\tlevel.Warn(db.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"Closing block failed\", \"err\", err, \"block\", ulid)\n  1660→\t\t\t}\n  1661→\t\t}\n  1662→\n  1663→\t\ttoDelete := filepath.Join(db.dir, ulid.String())\n  1664→\t\tswitch _, err := os.Stat(toDelete); {\n  1665→\t\tcase os.IsNotExist(err):\n  1666→\t\t\t// Noop.\n  1667→\t\t\tcontinue\n  1668→\t\tcase err != nil:\n  1669→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"stat dir %v: %w\", toDelete, err)\n  1670→\t\t}\n  1671→\n  1672→\t\t// Replace atomically to avoid partial block when process would crash during deletion.\n  1673→\t\ttmpToDelete := filepath.Join(db.dir, fmt.Sprintf(\"%s%s\", ulid, tmpForDeletionBlockDirSuffix))\n  1674→\t\tif err := fileutil.Replace(toDelete, tmpToDelete); err != nil {\n  1675→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"replace of obsolete block for deletion %s: %w\", ulid, err)\n  1676→\t\t}\n  1677→\t\tif err := os.RemoveAll(tmpToDelete); err != nil {\n  1678→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"delete obsolete block %s: %w\", ulid, err)\n  1679→\t\t}\n  1680→\t\tlevel.Info(db.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"Deleting obsolete block\", \"block\", ulid)\n  1681→\t}\n  1682→\n  1683→\treturn nil\n  1684→}\n  1685→\n  1686→// TimeRange specifies minTime and maxTime range.\n  1687→type TimeRange struct {\n  1688→\tMin, Max int64\n  1689→}\n  1690→\n  1691→// Overlaps contains overlapping blocks aggregated by overlapping range.\n  1692→type Overlaps map[TimeRange][]BlockMeta\n  1693→\n  1694→// String returns human readable string form of overlapped blocks.\n  1695→func (o Overlaps) String() string {\n  1696→\tvar res []string\n  1697→\tfor r, overlaps := range o {\n  1698→\t\tvar groups []string\n  1699→\t\tfor _, m := range overlaps {\n  1700→\t\t\tgroups = append(groups, fmt.Sprintf(\n  1701→\t\t\t\t\"<ulid: %s, mint: %d, maxt: %d, range: %s>\",\n  1702→\t\t\t\tm.ULID.String(),\n  1703→\t\t\t\tm.MinTime,\n  1704→\t\t\t\tm.MaxTime,\n  1705→\t\t\t\t(time.Duration((m.MaxTime-m.MinTime)/1000)*time.Second).String(),\n  1706→\t\t\t))\n  1707→\t\t}\n  1708→\t\tres = append(res, fmt.Sprintf(\n  1709→\t\t\t\"[mint: %d, maxt: %d, range: %s, blocks: %d]: %s\",\n  1710→\t\t\tr.Min, r.Max,\n  1711→\t\t\t(time.Duration((r.Max-r.Min)/1000)*time.Second).String(),\n  1712→\t\t\tlen(overlaps),\n  1713→\t\t\tstrings.Join(groups, \", \")),\n  1714→\t\t)\n  1715→\t}\n  1716→\treturn strings.Join(res, \"\\n\")\n  1717→}\n  1718→\n  1719→// OverlappingBlocks returns all overlapping blocks from given meta files.\n  1720→func OverlappingBlocks(bm []BlockMeta) Overlaps {\n  1721→\tif len(bm) <= 1 {\n  1722→\t\treturn nil\n  1723→\t}\n  1724→\tvar (\n  1725→\t\toverlaps [][]BlockMeta\n  1726→\n  1727→\t\t// pending contains not ended blocks in regards to \"current\" timestamp.\n  1728→\t\tpending = []BlockMeta{bm[0]}\n  1729→\t\t// continuousPending helps to aggregate same overlaps to single group.\n  1730→\t\tcontinuousPending = true\n  1731→\t)\n  1732→\n  1733→\t// We have here blocks sorted by minTime. We iterate over each block and treat its minTime as our \"current\" timestamp.\n  1734→\t// We check if any of the pending block finished (blocks that we have seen before, but their maxTime was still ahead current\n  1735→\t// timestamp). If not, it means they overlap with our current block. In the same time current block is assumed pending.\n  1736→\tfor _, b := range bm[1:] {\n  1737→\t\tvar newPending []BlockMeta\n  1738→\n  1739→\t\tfor _, p := range pending {\n  1740→\t\t\t// \"b.MinTime\" is our current time.\n  1741→\t\t\tif b.MinTime >= p.MaxTime {\n  1742→\t\t\t\tcontinuousPending = false\n  1743→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n  1744→\t\t\t}\n  1745→\n  1746→\t\t\t// \"p\" overlaps with \"b\" and \"p\" is still pending.\n  1747→\t\t\tnewPending = append(newPending, p)\n  1748→\t\t}\n  1749→\n  1750→\t\t// Our block \"b\" is now pending.\n  1751→\t\tpending = append(newPending, b)\n  1752→\t\tif len(newPending) == 0 {\n  1753→\t\t\t// No overlaps.\n  1754→\t\t\tcontinue\n  1755→\t\t}\n  1756→\n  1757→\t\tif continuousPending && len(overlaps) > 0 {\n  1758→\t\t\toverlaps[len(overlaps)-1] = append(overlaps[len(overlaps)-1], b)\n  1759→\t\t\tcontinue\n  1760→\t\t}\n  1761→\t\toverlaps = append(overlaps, append(newPending, b))\n  1762→\t\t// Start new pendings.\n  1763→\t\tcontinuousPending = true\n  1764→\t}\n  1765→\n  1766→\t// Fetch the critical overlapped time range foreach overlap groups.\n  1767→\toverlapGroups := Overlaps{}\n  1768→\tfor _, overlap := range overlaps {\n  1769→\t\tminRange := TimeRange{Min: 0, Max: math.MaxInt64}\n  1770→\t\tfor _, b := range overlap {\n  1771→\t\t\tif minRange.Max > b.MaxTime {\n  1772→\t\t\t\tminRange.Max = b.MaxTime\n  1773→\t\t\t}\n  1774→\n  1775→\t\t\tif minRange.Min < b.MinTime {\n  1776→\t\t\t\tminRange.Min = b.MinTime\n  1777→\t\t\t}\n  1778→\t\t}\n  1779→\t\toverlapGroups[minRange] = overlap\n  1780→\t}\n  1781→\n  1782→\treturn overlapGroups\n  1783→}\n  1784→\n  1785→func (db *DB) String() string {\n  1786→\treturn \"HEAD\"\n  1787→}\n  1788→\n  1789→// Blocks returns the databases persisted blocks.\n  1790→func (db *DB) Blocks() []*Block {\n  1791→\tdb.mtx.RLock()\n  1792→\tdefer db.mtx.RUnlock()\n  1793→\n  1794→\treturn db.blocks\n  1795→}\n  1796→\n  1797→// inOrderBlocksMaxTime returns the max time among the blocks that were not totally created\n  1798→// out of out-of-order data. If the returned boolean is true, it means there is at least\n  1799→// one such block.\n  1800→func (db *DB) inOrderBlocksMaxTime() (maxt int64, ok bool) {\n  1801→\tmaxt, ok = int64(math.MinInt64), false\n  1802→\t// If blocks are overlapping, last block might not have the max time. So check all blocks.\n  1803→\tfor _, b := range db.Blocks() {\n  1804→\t\tif !b.meta.Compaction.FromOutOfOrder() && b.meta.MaxTime > maxt {\n  1805→\t\t\tok = true\n  1806→\t\t\tmaxt = b.meta.MaxTime\n  1807→\t\t}\n  1808→\t}\n  1809→\treturn maxt, ok\n  1810→}\n  1811→\n  1812→// Head returns the databases's head.\n  1813→func (db *DB) Head() *Head {\n  1814→\treturn db.head\n  1815→}\n  1816→\n  1817→// Close the partition.\n  1818→func (db *DB) Close() error {\n  1819→\tclose(db.stopc)\n  1820→\tif db.compactCancel != nil {\n  1821→\t\tdb.compactCancel()\n  1822→\t}\n  1823→\t<-db.donec\n  1824→\n  1825→\tdb.mtx.Lock()\n  1826→\tdefer db.mtx.Unlock()\n  1827→\n  1828→\tvar g errgroup.Group\n  1829→\n  1830→\t// blocks also contains all head blocks.\n  1831→\tfor _, pb := range db.blocks {\n  1832→\t\tg.Go(pb.Close)\n  1833→\t}\n  1834→\n  1835→\terrs := tsdb_errors.NewMulti(g.Wait(), db.locker.Release())\n  1836→\tif db.head != nil {\n  1837→\t\terrs.Add(db.head.Close())\n  1838→\t}\n  1839→\treturn errs.Err()\n  1840→}\n  1841→\n  1842→// DisableCompactions disables auto compactions.\n  1843→func (db *DB) DisableCompactions() {\n  1844→\tdb.autoCompactMtx.Lock()\n  1845→\tdefer db.autoCompactMtx.Unlock()\n  1846→\n  1847→\tdb.autoCompact = false\n  1848→\tlevel.Info(db.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"Compactions disabled\")\n  1849→}\n  1850→\n  1851→// EnableCompactions enables auto compactions.\n  1852→func (db *DB) EnableCompactions() {\n  1853→\tdb.autoCompactMtx.Lock()\n  1854→\tdefer db.autoCompactMtx.Unlock()\n  1855→\n  1856→\tdb.autoCompact = true\n  1857→\tlevel.Info(db.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"Compactions enabled\")\n  1858→}\n  1859→\n  1860→// ForceHeadMMap is intended for use only in tests and benchmarks.\n  1861→func (db *DB) ForceHeadMMap() {\n  1862→\tdb.head.mmapHeadChunks()\n  1863→}\n  1864→\n  1865→// Snapshot writes the current data to the directory. If withHead is set to true it\n  1866→// will create a new block containing all data that's currently in the memory buffer/WAL.\n  1867→func (db *DB) Snapshot(dir string, withHead bool) error {\n  1868→\tif dir == db.dir {\n  1869→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"cannot snapshot into base directory\")\n  1870→\t}\n  1871→\tif _, err := ulid.ParseStrict(dir); err == nil {\n  1872→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"dir must not be a valid ULID\")\n  1873→\t}\n  1874→\n  1875→\tdb.cmtx.Lock()\n  1876→\tdefer db.cmtx.Unlock()\n  1877→\n  1878→\tdb.mtx.RLock()\n  1879→\tdefer db.mtx.RUnlock()\n  1880→\n  1881→\tfor _, b := range db.blocks {\n  1882→\t\tlevel.Info(db.logger).Log(\"msg\", \"Snapshotting block\", \"block\", b)\n  1883→\n  1884→\t\tif err := b.Snapshot(dir); err != nil {\n  1885→\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"error snapshotting block: %s: %w\", b.Dir(), err)\n  1886→\t\t}\n  1887→\t}\n  1888→\tif !withHead {\n  1889→\t\treturn nil\n  1890→\t}\n  1891→\n  1892→\tmint := db.head.MinTime()\n  1893→\tmaxt := db.head.MaxTime()\n  1894→\thead := NewRangeHead(db.head, mint, maxt)\n  1895→\t// Add +1 millisecond to block maxt because block intervals are half-open: [b.MinTime, b.MaxTime).\n  1896→\t// Because of this block intervals are always +1 than the total samples it includes.\n  1897→\tif _, err := db.compactor.Write(dir, head, mint, maxt+1, nil); err != nil {\n  1898→\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"snapshot head block: %w\", err)\n  1899→\t}\n  1900→\treturn nil\n  1901→}\n  1902→\n  1903→// Querier returns a new querier over the data partition for the given time range.\n  1904→func (db *DB) Querier(mint, maxt int64) (_ storage.Querier, err error) {\n  1905→\tvar blocks []BlockReader\n  1906→\n  1907→\tdb.mtx.RLock()\n  1908→\tdefer db.mtx.RUnlock()\n  1909→\n  1910→\tfor _, b := range db.blocks {\n  1911→\t\tif b.OverlapsClosedInterval(mint, maxt) {\n  1912→\t\t\tblocks = append(blocks, b)\n  1913→\t\t}\n  1914→\t}\n  1915→\n  1916→\tblockQueriers := make([]storage.Querier, 0, len(blocks)+2) // +2 to allow for possible in-order and OOO head queriers\n  1917→\n  1918→\tdefer func() {\n  1919→\t\tif err != nil {\n  1920→\t\t\t// If we fail, all previously opened queriers must be closed.\n  1921→\t\t\tfor _, q := range blockQueriers {\n  1922→\t\t\t\t// TODO(bwplotka): Handle error.\n  1923→\t\t\t\t_ = q.Close()\n  1924→\t\t\t}\n  1925→\t\t}\n  1926→\t}()\n  1927→\n  1928→\tif maxt >= db.head.MinTime() {\n  1929→\t\trh := NewRangeHead(db.head, mint, maxt)\n  1930→\t\tvar err error\n  1931→\t\tinOrderHeadQuerier, err := NewBlockQuerier(rh, mint, maxt)\n  1932→\t\tif err != nil {\n  1933→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"open block querier for head %s: %w\", rh, err)\n  1934→\t\t}\n  1935→\n  1936→\t\t// Getting the querier above registers itself in the queue that the truncation waits on.\n  1937→\t\t// So if the querier is currently not colliding with any truncation, we can continue to use it and still\n  1938→\t\t// won't run into a race later since any truncation that comes after will wait on this querier if it overlaps.\n  1939→\t\tshouldClose, getNew, newMint := db.head.IsQuerierCollidingWithTruncation(mint, maxt)\n  1940→\t\tif shouldClose {\n  1941→\t\t\tif err := inOrderHeadQuerier.Close(); err != nil {\n  1942→\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"closing head block querier %s: %w\", rh, err)\n  1943→\t\t\t}\n  1944→\t\t\tinOrderHeadQuerier = nil\n  1945→\t\t}\n  1946→\t\tif getNew {\n  1947→\t\t\trh := NewRangeHead(db.head, newMint, maxt)\n  1948→\t\t\tinOrderHeadQuerier, err = NewBlockQuerier(rh, newMint, maxt)\n  1949→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n  1950→\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"open block querier for head while getting new querier %s: %w\", rh, err)\n  1951→\t\t\t}\n  1952→\t\t}\n  1953→\n  1954→\t\tif inOrderHeadQuerier != nil {\n  1955→\t\t\tblockQueriers = append(blockQueriers, inOrderHeadQuerier)\n  1956→\t\t}\n  1957→\t}\n  1958→\n  1959→\tif overlapsClosedInterval(mint, maxt, db.head.MinOOOTime(), db.head.MaxOOOTime()) {\n  1960→\t\trh := NewOOORangeHead(db.head, mint, maxt, db.lastGarbageCollectedMmapRef)\n  1961→\t\tvar err error\n  1962→\t\toutOfOrderHeadQuerier, err := NewBlockQuerier(rh, mint, maxt)\n  1963→\t\tif err != nil {\n  1964→\t\t\t// If NewBlockQuerier() failed, make sure to clean up the pending read created by NewOOORangeHead.\n  1965→\t\t\trh.isoState.Close()\n  1966→\n  1967→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"open block querier for ooo head %s: %w\", rh, err)\n  1968→\t\t}\n  1969→\n  1970→\t\tblockQueriers = append(blockQueriers, outOfOrderHeadQuerier)\n  1971→\t}\n  1972→\n  1973→\tfor _, b := range blocks {\n  1974→\t\tq, err := NewBlockQuerier(b, mint, maxt)\n  1975→\t\tif err != nil {\n  1976→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"open querier for block %s: %w\", b, err)\n  1977→\t\t}\n  1978→\t\tblockQueriers = append(blockQueriers, q)\n  1979→\t}\n  1980→\n  1981→\treturn storage.NewMergeQuerier(blockQueriers, nil, storage.ChainedSeriesMerge), nil\n  1982→}\n  1983→\n  1984→// blockChunkQuerierForRange returns individual block chunk queriers from the persistent blocks, in-order head block, and the\n  1985→// out-of-order head block, overlapping with the given time range.\n  1986→func (db *DB) blockChunkQuerierForRange(mint, maxt int64) (_ []storage.ChunkQuerier, err error) {\n  1987→\tvar blocks []BlockReader\n  1988→\n  1989→\tdb.mtx.RLock()\n  1990→\tdefer db.mtx.RUnlock()\n  1991→\n  1992→\tfor _, b := range db.blocks {\n  1993→\t\tif b.OverlapsClosedInterval(mint, maxt) {\n  1994→\t\t\tblocks = append(blocks, b)\n  1995→\t\t}\n  1996→\t}\n  1997→\n  1998→\tblockQueriers := make([]storage.ChunkQuerier, 0, len(blocks)+2) // +2 to allow for possible in-order and OOO head queriers\n  1999→\n  2000→\tdefer func() {\n  2001→\t\tif err != nil {\n  2002→\t\t\t// If we fail, all previously opened queriers must be closed.\n  2003→\t\t\tfor _, q := range blockQueriers {\n  2004→\t\t\t\t// TODO(bwplotka): Handle error.\n  2005→\t\t\t\t_ = q.Close()\n  2006→\t\t\t}\n  2007→\t\t}\n  2008→\t}()\n  2009→\n  2010→\tif maxt >= db.head.MinTime() {\n  2011→\t\trh := NewRangeHead(db.head, mint, maxt)\n  2012→\t\tinOrderHeadQuerier, err := NewBlockChunkQuerier(rh, mint, maxt)\n  2013→\t\tif err != nil {\n  2014→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"open querier for head %s: %w\", rh, err)\n  2015→\t\t}\n  2016→\n  2017→\t\t// Getting the querier above registers itself in the queue that the truncation waits on.\n  2018→\t\t// So if the querier is currently not colliding with any truncation, we can continue to use it and still\n  2019→\t\t// won't run into a race later since any truncation that comes after will wait on this querier if it overlaps.\n  2020→\t\tshouldClose, getNew, newMint := db.head.IsQuerierCollidingWithTruncation(mint, maxt)\n  2021→\t\tif shouldClose {\n  2022→\t\t\tif err := inOrderHeadQuerier.Close(); err != nil {\n  2023→\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"closing head querier %s: %w\", rh, err)\n  2024→\t\t\t}\n  2025→\t\t\tinOrderHeadQuerier = nil\n  2026→\t\t}\n  2027→\t\tif getNew {\n  2028→\t\t\trh := NewRangeHead(db.head, newMint, maxt)\n  2029→\t\t\tinOrderHeadQuerier, err = NewBlockChunkQuerier(rh, newMint, maxt)\n  2030→\t\t\tif err != nil {\n  2031→\t\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"open querier for head while getting new querier %s: %w\", rh, err)\n  2032→\t\t\t}\n  2033→\t\t}\n  2034→\n  2035→\t\tif inOrderHeadQuerier != nil {\n  2036→\t\t\tblockQueriers = append(blockQueriers, inOrderHeadQuerier)\n  2037→\t\t}\n  2038→\t}\n  2039→\n  2040→\tif overlapsClosedInterval(mint, maxt, db.head.MinOOOTime(), db.head.MaxOOOTime()) {\n  2041→\t\trh := NewOOORangeHead(db.head, mint, maxt, db.lastGarbageCollectedMmapRef)\n  2042→\t\toutOfOrderHeadQuerier, err := NewBlockChunkQuerier(rh, mint, maxt)\n  2043→\t\tif err != nil {\n  2044→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"open block chunk querier for ooo head %s: %w\", rh, err)\n  2045→\t\t}\n  2046→\n  2047→\t\tblockQueriers = append(blockQueriers, outOfOrderHeadQuerier)\n  2048→\t}\n  2049→\n  2050→\tfor _, b := range blocks {\n  2051→\t\tq, err := NewBlockChunkQuerier(b, mint, maxt)\n  2052→\t\tif err != nil {\n  2053→\t\t\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\"open querier for block %s: %w\", b, err)\n  2054→\t\t}\n  2055→\t\tblockQueriers = append(blockQueriers, q)\n  2056→\t}\n  2057→\n  2058→\treturn blockQueriers, nil\n  2059→}\n  2060→\n  2061→// ChunkQuerier returns a new chunk querier over the data partition for the given time range.\n  2062→func (db *DB) ChunkQuerier(mint, maxt int64) (storage.ChunkQuerier, error) {\n  2063→\tblockQueriers, err := db.blockChunkQuerierForRange(mint, maxt)\n  2064→\tif err != nil {\n  2065→\t\treturn nil, err\n  2066→\t}\n  2067→\treturn storage.NewMergeChunkQuerier(blockQueriers, nil, storage.NewCompactingChunkSeriesMerger(storage.ChainedSeriesMerge)), nil\n  2068→}\n  2069→\n  2070→func (db *DB) ExemplarQuerier(ctx context.Context) (storage.ExemplarQuerier, error) {\n  2071→\treturn db.head.exemplars.ExemplarQuerier(ctx)\n  2072→}\n  2073→\n  2074→func rangeForTimestamp(t, width int64) (maxt int64) {\n  2075→\treturn (t/width)*width + width\n  2076→}\n  2077→\n  2078→// Delete implements deletion of metrics. It only has atomicity guarantees on a per-block basis.\n  2079→func (db *DB) Delete(ctx context.Context, mint, maxt int64, ms ...*labels.Matcher) error {\n  2080→\tdb.cmtx.Lock()\n  2081→\tdefer db.cmtx.Unlock()\n  2082→\n  2083→\tvar g errgroup.Group\n  2084→\n  2085→\tdb.mtx.RLock()\n  2086→\tdefer db.mtx.RUnlock()\n  2087→\n  2088→\tfor _, b := range db.blocks {\n  2089→\t\tif b.OverlapsClosedInterval(mint, maxt) {\n  2090→\t\t\tg.Go(func(b *Block) func() error {\n  2091→\t\t\t\treturn func() error { return b.Delete(ctx, mint, maxt, ms...) }\n  2092→\t\t\t}(b))\n  2093→\t\t}\n  2094→\t}\n  2095→\tif db.head.OverlapsClosedInterval(mint, maxt) {\n  2096→\t\tg.Go(func() error {\n  2097→\t\t\treturn db.head.Delete(ctx, mint, maxt, ms...)\n  2098→\t\t})\n  2099→\t}\n  2100→\n  2101→\treturn g.Wait()\n  2102→}\n  2103→\n  2104→// CleanTombstones re-writes any blocks with tombstones.\n  2105→func (db *DB) CleanTombstones() (err error) {\n  2106→\tdb.cmtx.Lock()\n  2107→\tdefer db.cmtx.Unlock()\n  2108→\n  2109→\tstart := time.Now()\n  2110→\tdefer func() {\n  2111→\t\tdb.metrics.tombCleanTimer.Observe(time.Since(start).Seconds())\n  2112→\t}()\n  2113→\n  2114→\tcleanUpCompleted := false\n  2115→\t// Repeat cleanup until there is no tombstones left.\n  2116→\tfor !cleanUpCompleted {\n  2117→\t\tcleanUpCompleted = true\n  2118→\n  2119→\t\tfor _, pb := range db.Blocks() {\n  2120→\t\t\tuid, safeToDelete, cleanErr := pb.CleanTombstones(db.Dir(), db.compactor)\n  2121→\t\t\tif cleanErr != nil {\n  2122→\t\t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"clean tombstones: %s: %w\", pb.Dir(), cleanErr)\n  2123→\t\t\t}\n  2124→\t\t\tif !safeToDelete {\n  2125→\t\t\t\t// There was nothing to clean.\n  2126→\t\t\t\tcontinue\n  2127→\t\t\t}\n  2128→\n  2129→\t\t\t// In case tombstones of the old block covers the whole block,\n  2130→\t\t\t// then there would be no resultant block to tell the parent.\n  2131→\t\t\t// The lock protects against race conditions when deleting blocks\n  2132→\t\t\t// during an already running reload.\n  2133→\t\t\tdb.mtx.Lock()\n  2134→\t\t\tpb.meta.Compaction.Deletable = safeToDelete\n  2135→\t\t\tdb.mtx.Unlock()\n  2136→\t\t\tcleanUpCompleted = false\n  2137→\t\t\tif err = db.reloadBlocks(); err == nil { // Will try to delete old block.\n  2138→\t\t\t\t// Successful reload will change the existing blocks.\n  2139→\t\t\t\t// We need to loop over the new set of blocks.\n  2140→\t\t\t\tbreak\n  2141→\t\t\t}\n  2142→\n  2143→\t\t\t// Delete new block if it was created.\n  2144→\t\t\tif uid != nil && *uid != (ulid.ULID{}) {\n  2145→\t\t\t\tdir := filepath.Join(db.Dir(), uid.String())\n  2146→\t\t\t\tif err := os.RemoveAll(dir); err != nil {\n
